- **The professional finish over the unchanged core** — tradecraft polishes across the period; cruelty does not.
- **The mask-as-face** — completed at the disfigurement; symbol fully replaces self.
- **The peer-bond exception (Sin)** — the one horizontal-coded relationship in the file, permitted only by her vertical authorization.
- **The voice-register tell** — short, formal, profanity-free when Skull-line is psychologically present; loose and obscene otherwise. Most reliable internal-state indicator the file has.
- **The route discipline** — no repeated routes within thirty days; vetted drivers only; early arrival and surveillance at meeting sites; self-assembled ordnance.
- **The sleep pattern** — four-to-five-hour increments; transit-sleep capability; instant wake; no reportable dream content.
- **The affect floor** — no depression, no anxiety, no remorse, no PTSD; the only documented affect-disregulator is threat to or contempt for the Skull-line.

The middle period is, in the end, the period in which the subject *became finished*. He entered it as a high-end Skull-aligned enforcer with twenty years of street and academy work behind him. He exits it as a fully consolidated symbol — masked, partnered to the Skull-line's heir, owner of the most consequential single kill on his ledger, and proof against every form of psychological pressure that the apparatus opposing him knew how to apply. The late-period record will show no further evolution of the man. Only the deployments change.

— END SECTION; CONTINUE TO CHRONOLOGY IV (LATE PERIOD: STANDOFF, PLEASANT HILL, SECRET EMPIRE, AND THE TERMINAL DEPLOYMENTS).


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

## SUBJECT: BROCK RUMLOW (CROSSBONES)
### Period Covered: Standoff (early 2016) → Present
### Classification: Behavioral reconstruction, longitudinal — continuous-surveillance equivalent

---

## A. The Pleasant Hill Interval (Standoff, early 2016)

The recent-history arc opens not with an act but with an *absence*. Subject is removed from the operational theater and inserted, against his will and without his knowledge, into the Kobik-generated containment community of **Pleasant Hill, Connecticut** — a SHIELD black-program prison disguised as a suburban town, in which Cosmic Cube fragments rewrite inmate identities into civilian personas.

Inside Pleasant Hill, Rumlow is reconstituted as a soft-bodied middle-aged man with a vaguely service-industry life, no memory of Crossbones, no memory of the Skull, no memory of disfigurement. The face under the mask is restored; the mask itself is gone. He moves through the town's diner-and-driveway choreography with the affect of a man who has never killed anyone. **This is the only documented period in the subject's adult life in which he is not, behaviorally, Brock Rumlow.** It is also, behaviorally, the most diagnostically clarifying period in the file: the Kobik substrate strips away everything *organized around* the sadistic core and reveals what is left when the organizing structures are dissolved. What is left is *thin* — a generic citizen with no apparent inner life, no hobbies, no curiosities, no longings. The civilian Rumlow is not a person hiding under the soldier; he is a husk. This corroborates the §3 finding that the violence is not a defense against an inner self, because there is no inner self underneath; the violence *is* the self.

When the Pleasant Hill containment ruptures and inmates begin to remember, Rumlow's return to baseline is not gradual. The reawakening is described in the record as switch-like: the mild posture, the slack jaw, the unhurried gait, all gone in seconds, replaced by tactical body-set and the cold register that is his neutral. He does not appear to experience the period of imprisonment as a loss (which would imply the civilian life had been preferable in some way); he experiences it as a theft of *time on mission*. No revenge cathexis attaches to Maria Hill personally despite Hill being the architect. The grievance is filed under *interference with the work*, not personal violation. This is consistent.

He is among the inmates who escape during the Standoff fracas. He returns to operational tempo within days.

---

## B. The Pre-Empire Period (Spring–Summer 2016)

In the months between Pleasant Hill and **Secret Empire**, Subject rebuilds. The reconstruction is methodical and reveals the granular habits of his re-entry pattern, which the file has now observed three separate times across the published record (post-disfigurement, post-Fear Itself dispersals, post-Pleasant Hill). The sequence is invariant:

1. **Acquire mask first, weapons second, lodging third.** The Crossbones tactical mask — or a serviceable replacement — is sourced before any other operational gear. He cannot conduct business as Rumlow-the-face for more than the minimum hours required.
2. **Reestablish the Skull-line link.** In this cycle, the Skull-line is represented by the Red Skull's encrypted command channels and, downstream, by the cell architecture being assembled by the Skull/Hydra-Cap operation. Subject does not freelance in this interval. He does not take outside contracts. He does not generate income from non-aligned employers. This is unusual for a mercenary of his caliber and is the cleanest single demonstration that he is *not* a mercenary in motive — he is a soldier waiting for orders from a specific army.
3. **Re-cultivate Sin.** Contact with Sinthea Schmidt is re-established as part of, not separate from, item 2. Their reunion is reported in the record as warm by Rumlow's standards — meaning physically close, operationally collaborative, sexually resumed. No documented quarrel about the lost time. They pick up.
4. **Resume conditioning.** Within two weeks of operational re-entry the physical baseline has been recovered. The Pleasant Hill body — softer, slower, civilian-fed — is gone. This is observable in surveillance imagery: posture realigned, gait shortened and balanced, weight redistributed forward over the balls of the feet, hands kept loose at hip level rather than at sides.

The relevant inference: Rumlow does not require *recovery time*. He requires re-equipping time. The personality is impact-resistant in a way the body is not.

---

## C. The Hydra-Captain America Operation (Secret Empire, 2017)

This is the most behaviorally interesting chapter of the recent record, because it tests — and confirms — the central analytic claim of §5: that Subject's organizing object is the **Skull-line / Skull-project**, not any individual person, and that the loyalty migrates wherever the project moves.

In Secret Empire, the Red Skull's long-running operation to rewrite Steve Rogers into a Hydra Supreme Leader bears fruit. Rogers, his personal history overwritten by Kobik on the Skull's behalf, *is* the Skull's product even when he subsequently betrays and discards the Skull personally. Rumlow's response to this configuration is the single cleanest behavioral demonstration of his structural psychology yet recorded.

He serves Hydra-Cap.

Without hesitation. Without ideological adjustment. Without, apparently, requiring any explanation. The man who killed Steve Rogers on the courthouse steps in 2007 now takes orders from a man wearing Steve Rogers's face and body, and the transition produces no observable cognitive dissonance. The file's reading: Rumlow does not perceive himself to have switched sides. From his standpoint there was never a side called "Steve Rogers" or a side called "Hydra-Cap"; there was only the Skull's project, in which Rogers was first an obstacle to be eliminated and is now a vessel to be served. The vessel changed; the project did not.

Operational role across the Empire arc:
- Deployed as enforcement muscle within the post-takeover security architecture, but *not* placed in the upper command tier. This is correct allocation by Hydra leadership and is also consistent with Rumlow's self-concept — he does not appear to lobby for elevation. He is the right hand and prefers it.
- Used in interrogation and reprisal operations against captured resistance figures. Behavioral note: in this period the sadistic component is observed at *elevated* tempo relative to baseline. With Hydra ascendant and the constraint against open cruelty lifted, Rumlow's discretionary violence widens. He kills more, slower, and with more visible enjoyment in this window than in any comparably documented period.
- Maintains the partnership with Sin in parallel; their joint operations during the Empire period are coordinated and effective.

When the Hydra-Cap edifice collapses and the real Rogers is restored, Rumlow does not surrender, does not apologize, does not reorient. He fights, then withdraws. There is no recorded post-collapse depressive interval. The project has receded *again*; the soldier *waits again*.

---

## D. The Post-Empire Diaspora (late 2017 onward)

This is the period during which the published record on Subject becomes intermittent rather than continuous — a function less of his diminished activity than of the narrative center of gravity shifting to other Captain America–adjacent figures. From an intelligence standpoint, intermittent reporting on a target of this typology is *not* reassuring; Rumlow's operational tempo does not require headlines.

Documented and inferable activity in this period:

- **Sporadic enforcement work** on behalf of the residual Hydra cell network and Skull-aligned operations. He does not appear to have rebuilt a personal cell of comparable size to the pre-Empire era. He works in pairs, trios, sometimes alone.
- **Continued partnership with Sin** where she surfaces; periods of separation when her operations diverge geographically. Subject does not appear to suffer separation from Sin in the manner he would suffer separation from the Skull-cause itself. She is partner-and-Skull-surrogate, but she is *not* the organizing object — she is its current avatar. The discrimination matters and is borne out by his behavior: he tolerates her absence; he does not tolerate the cause's absence.
- **Confrontations with Sam Wilson, Bucky Barnes, and the broader Cap-legacy axis** during opportunistic encounters. The Wilson encounters are particularly revealing: Rumlow's contempt register, ordinarily reserved for Rogers's "softness," extends to Wilson on different grounds — Wilson, in Rumlow's reading, is an *unauthorized claimant* to the symbol, and Rumlow's hostility toward him carries a racial-supremacist coloration consistent with the Skull-line ideology he has absorbed. The file notes this not as a new ideological development but as the foreground emergence of a background datum: Rumlow's fascism, never philosophically articulated by him, has always been operationally complete, racial axis included.
- **Recurrent reported deaths** and returns. The published record contains multiple kill-confirmed sequences for Subject across the post-Empire years; in every documented case the death is partial, delayed, or reversed. The file treats Rumlow as functionally non-confirmable as deceased absent direct biometric corroboration over a sustained period. Operationally: *assume alive*.

---

## E. Body, Face, and the Mask — Current Somatic State

Estimated chronological age in the published-record present: mid-to-late forties, possibly early fifties depending on which timeline conversion is applied. Functional combat age: indistinguishable from a disciplined operator a decade younger, owing to conditioning, possible residual serum-derivative augmentation from the Brubaker-era exposures, and an injury-management posture that the subject's pain tolerance permits him to maintain without pharmacological assistance.

**Face.** The burn scarring persists. There is no record of reconstructive intervention; the file's reading is that he has refused such intervention even when access has been available. The face under the mask is, by this point, an artifact he has had longer than the unburned face he originally lost — closing in on, or past, the temporal midpoint. The mask is no longer a covering of a face; the face *under* the mask is the relic, and the mask is the public artifact.

**Body.** Heavily scarred across torso, arms, thighs — the cumulative record of three decades of frontline operations. Tattoo work present from the Crims-era and accreted over the years; a partial skull motif across the chest is documented, predating the persona name and arguably one of its sources. Posture: shoulders forward, hands at hip, weight on the balls of the feet — the field-ready stance is his resting stance.

**Pain.** Chronic neuropathic facial pain and chronic musculoskeletal pain are presumed continuous. Subject's management of this pain is, per §4, *personality-congruent denial* — he does not report it, does not medicate for it, and appears to integrate it as a background tonic of bodily existence. The hypothesis the file has tested across multiple windows is that the chronic pain functions for him as a *constant subliminal reminder of injury done to him by the enemy*, and thus as a low-grade affective fuel source for the work. Removing the pain — were it possible — might actually degrade his motivational baseline. He should not, on this reading, be treated medically against his stated preference; the pain is operationally load-bearing for him.

**Voice.** Damage to the lower face and jaw musculature has rendered his voice rougher and lower-pitched than the pre-burn baseline. He uses this. The vocal register is now part of the terror-aesthetic.

---

## F. Current Behavioral Routines (Reconstructed)

The file's reconstruction of Subject's present-day weekly pattern, derived from cross-era invariants and recent-era observations:

- **Sleep:** short, broken, tactical. Five to six hours, rarely contiguous; wakes fully alert. Sleeps armed.
- **Conditioning:** daily, twice. Morning circuit emphasizing explosive output and grip; evening session emphasizing edged-weapon flow drills, often with a partner if Sin or a trusted subordinate is on-station. Heavy bag work several times weekly.
- **Range time:** weekly minimum, often more. Mixed long arm and sidearm. Subject is documented across the entire record as a meticulous maintainer of his own weapons; he does not delegate cleaning or zeroing.
- **Communications:** disciplined. Single-use devices; brief calls. He does not maintain online social presence. He does not write.
- **Reading:** none of consequence in the record. He does not appear to read for pleasure or instruction. Operational documents, target packets, after-action reports — only.
- **Eating:** unfussy, high-protein, large quantities. No documented dietary preference or restriction beyond performance considerations.
- **Sexual activity:** with Sin when co-located. Outside that partnership, the record contains coercive episodes but no sustained alternative attachment. The file's working assumption is that opportunistic encounters occur but are not relationally weighted.
- **Off-duty behavior:** there is essentially no documented off-duty behavior. Subject does not appear to have hobbies, civilian friendships, recreational pursuits, or any non-operational social geometry. Pleasant Hill confirmed what the prior file had inferred: the civilian register is not merely suppressed, it is *empty*.

---

## G. Current Affiliations and Dependencies

- **The Skull-line / Skull-project:** organizing object, undiminished. Specific incarnations have rotated (the original Red Skull, the Schmidt-clone variants, Sin-as-Skadi, Hydra-Cap-as-Skull-product), but the cathexis to the line itself is the longest-running and most stable attachment in his life. **Current status of dependency: total.** Disruption of this dependency remains the single most powerful potential intervention point against him.
- **Sin (Sinthea Schmidt):** primary peer-coded relationship, partner-and-Skull-surrogate. Operationally fluctuating co-presence; affectively stable. Threats to Sin remain the most reliable single tactical-decompensation trigger.
- **Hydra residual networks:** present, fractured, opportunistically utilized. Not loyalty objects in themselves; vessels for the project.
- **No civilian dependencies of any kind:** no documented physician, no documented attorney other than mission-attached counsel, no documented financial advisor, no real estate held in his own name, no vehicle registered in his own name, no recurring civilian service relationships. He is, in the modern surveillance sense, *deliberately illegible* — a man with no civilian footprint to map.

---

## H. Where He Is Now, and How He Got There

The trajectory from the disfigurement (c. 2009 in publishing time) to the present is a single sustained line with a brief Kobik-induced interruption: a man who organized his life around being the right hand of an authoritarian father-figure, lost the face he had been born with, replaced it with the symbol he had been building toward anyway, served the father-figure through the father-figure's death and resurrection and proxy embodiments, served the daughter when she became the Hammer-bearer, served the proxy-Steve when the project temporarily moved into that body, and on the project's collapse withdrew to wait for the next vessel without any apparent reconstitution of self required.

He is, in the published-record present, **operationally active, intermittently visible, partnered with Sin when geography permits, between large-scale operations, and waiting**. The waiting is not idle; it is filled with conditioning, small-scale enforcement, and the slow accretion of cell architecture for whatever the next Skull-aligned move requires. He has not aged out. He has not been rehabilitated. He has not been redeemed by relationship, by injury, by imprisonment, by the temporary erasure of his identity, or by the betrayal of his cause by its own leadership. None of the conventional narrative engines that turn villains have purchased traction on him. This is the empirical finding of the recent-history window and it should not be wished away.

The current dossier conclusion is unchanged from §5: leverage against Subject is not psychological excavation. It is **displacement, corruption, or visible squandering of the organizing object**. Everything else — bodily injury, captivity, identity-erasure, ideological discredit at a distance — has now been tested against him in the recent window and has failed to produce structural change. He is durable in exactly the way a personality so completely organized around an external authoritarian object is durable: he cannot be broken from within because the within is small. He can only be unmade from without, and only by taking the object away in a manner he cannot reframe as temporary.

Until then: assume continuous low-tempo operational readiness. Assume the mask is on. Assume he is armed. Assume he is waiting for the next vessel of the Skull-line to surface, and that when it does, he will move toward it within hours.

— END SECTION. CONTINUES IN PART V.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: BROCK RUMLOW

*File segment M-1 through M-9. Reconstructed from operational footage, captured-combatant medical intake records (SHIELD custody 2007, 2010, 2016), open-source forensic imaging, recovered Hydra biometric logs, and behavioral inference where direct records are unavailable. Where the record is silent, gaps are flagged.*

---

## M-1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

Subject presents, at operational peak (estimated ages 28–42), as a male of approximately 6'1" (185 cm), lean operational mass cycling between 220–245 lb (100–111 kg) depending on enhancement phase, mesomorphic with hypertrophied trapezius/deltoid/latissimus development consistent with decades of weighted carry, climbing, and breach work rather than aesthetic lifting. Resting heart rate, inferred from observed recovery intervals between exertional bouts (rappel-to-fire sequences during the Federal Courthouse operation, multi-room CQB clearances during the Pleasant Hill breakout), almost certainly sits in the high-40s to low-50s — elite-operator cardiovascular conditioning sustained well past the age at which most field personnel decline.

Resting respiratory pattern is diaphragmatic and slow; he has been observed to control his breathing audibly through the rebreather grille of the mask under conditions where untrained personnel would hyperventilate (the Empire State subway pursuit; the Madripoor exfil). Pupillary response is unremarkable in the absence of enhancement compounds — flat, slow, baseline-aggressive rather than baseline-anxious. Skin tone before disfigurement: olive-Mediterranean, indoor-pale during prolonged Hydra installation tours, weathered during desert and tropical operations. Right-hand dominant; can shoot a long arm off either shoulder, can knife-fight off either lead — a Taskmaster-academy hallmark.

Dental: previously good, with two crowns on the lower-right molars (inferred from a 2006 Bahrain medical chit recovered post-operation) almost certainly secondary to fight trauma rather than dental caries. Post-disfigurement, dental status presumed unchanged but inaccessible without removal of facial prosthetic; the mask architecture permits chewing and swallowing.

---

## M-2. THE PRE-RECORD INJURY LAYER (Adolescence, Lower East Side)

No formal medical record exists for the Savage Crims era. Behavioral and somatic markers, however, encode it. The subject moves with a slight favor of the left hip on long marches — consistent with an old, untreated greater-trochanteric or sacroiliac injury, the kind a teenager takes in a stairwell beating and does not present to a clinic. The bridge of the nose, visible in pre-disfigurement photographs, shows two distinct healed deviations, neither surgically corrected: at least two broken-nose events before age twenty, set without reduction. Brow ridge scarring (left supraorbital, approximately 2 cm; right, smaller, more recent) consistent with bare-knuckle exchange. A thin linear scar along the right mandibular angle — knife graze, healed without sutures.

These are the somatic fossils of the origin period. They establish a critical baseline: the subject entered professional violence already pre-conditioned to absorb and ignore injury without medical mediation. This is not a man who learned to tolerate pain in training; he arrived tolerant.

---

## M-3. THE TASKMASTER-ACADEMY PERIOD AND PROFESSIONALIZATION

Roughly ages 18–22. Medical record remains absent (the academy operated without official documentation), but the body learned to file injuries. Inferred from later operational profile:

- **Repetitive joint micro-trauma** — shoulders (rotator cuff stress from heavy-bag and weapon-retention drills), knees (descending-stair and rooftop landings), wrists (blade-on-blade impact). Established the chronic-tendinopathy pattern that he will manage by deliberate warm-up rituals visible across his later career.
- **First documented gunshot wound** (Taskmaster academy graduating exercise, per Skull-side debrief excerpts later recovered): through-and-through, lateral right thigh, missed femur and femoral artery. Healed with a palpable ridge of scar tissue and a subtle gait compensation he eventually trained out.
- **Acquisition of pain-management discipline.** The defining medical fact of this period is *not* an injury but a learned skill: he developed the operator's capacity to sustain function through Grade-II/III injuries that would remove a normal patient from duty. Clinically, this is dissociative analgesia under voluntary control, a trait that overlaps the psychopathy literature on diminished pain reactivity.

Psychological impact of the academy-period injuries: **none observable.** No avoidance behaviors, no superstition around the wounded areas, no compensatory equipment fetish. The wounds are filed as data, not as story.

---

## M-4. THE FIELD-COMMANDER ERA — CUMULATIVE COMBAT INJURY (~ages 22–38)

This is the densest single section of the medical record and necessarily the most reconstructive.

**Gunshot wounds, lifetime, conservative estimate: 9–14.** Documented or strongly inferable from on-panel evidence:
- Left shoulder, through-and-through (engagement with Diamondback's Serpent Society allies); managed in the field, never properly debrided; produces a small residual range-of-motion deficit in overhead reach with left arm.
- Right flank, oblique, glancing rib (Punisher engagement, 1990s, off-record); fractured 9th rib, healed with callus.
- Lower-left abdomen, near miss on descending colon; required surgical intervention at a Hydra-aligned facility; healed adhesion burden likely produces episodic abdominal discomfort he ignores.
- Right calf (Bucky Barnes engagement, Brubaker Cap arc); muscle through-and-through, no neurovascular involvement.
- Two further wounds attributed to SHIELD strike-team engagements; locations: right deltoid, left buttock.
- Cluster of fragment wounds across upper back from a flashbang/grenade exchange (Latveria peripheral op); embedded micro-fragments likely remain.

**Edged-weapon trauma.** Multiple healed lacerations across the forearms (defensive cuts), one across the left palm with partial flexor tendon involvement that he rehabilitated to full function; a long oblique scar across the lower abdomen (origin unrecovered); shallow puncture scar over the right pectoral.

**Blunt-impact and skeletal injury.** Documented or inferable fractures: left zygomatic arch (healed with subtle asymmetry detectable in pre-disfigurement imaging); right ulna midshaft (healed straight, suggesting reduction by a competent if unofficial provider); two finger fractures (right 4th and 5th metacarpals — boxer's fractures); compression-grade vertebral injury at approximately T7-T9 from a high-fall event (rooftop drop during the Diamondback abduction sequence), producing a slight kyphotic set he carries to this day. Bilateral knee meniscal degeneration consistent with operational load over decades.

**Blast and barotrauma.** Repeated exposure to breaching charges, grenades, and one significant exposure to an Asgardian-origin energy discharge during the Fear Itself sequence. Almost certain low-grade chronic tinnitus; partial high-frequency hearing loss bilaterally, more pronounced on the right (lead-side ear for long-arm shooting). He compensates by positioning interlocutors and by lip-reading in noise — a behavior visible if one watches him in crowded operational environments.

**Mild-to-moderate cumulative TBI burden.** Multiple concussive events from blast, blunt impact, and falls. Behaviorally, no gross deficit; subtly, he runs slightly hot in his late thirties and forties — the patience that defines him at his best wears thinner more quickly after exertion, and his sleep architecture (inferred from surveillance of bivouac patterns) is fragmented in the second half of the night. These are non-specific markers consistent with chronic-trauma encephalopathy in its sub-syndromal range. He will never be diagnosed; the diagnosis would not change his conduct.

**Psychological impact, cumulative.** *Negligible in any standard sense.* He neither catastrophizes injury nor minimizes it for performance reasons — he files it accurately and proceeds. Crucially, there is **no evidence of injury-driven avoidance, no superstitious routine around prior wound sites, no startle response degradation**. The body, to him, is materiel. When materiel degrades, you compensate or you replace.

---

## M-5. ENHANCEMENT EPISODES

The subject is **not** a super-soldier in the Rogers sense, and he is **not** a stable enhanced — but he has crossed the enhancement threshold more than once.

**Episode A — Derivative serum exposure (Brubaker era).** A Skull-supplied derivative compound, almost certainly a Hydra-iterated Erskine analogue, was administered prior to the Federal Courthouse operation and at least one subsequent engagement. Effects observed: measurable increase in striking power (he hand-throws an adult male across a room in one recovered fragment), tolerance for ballistic impact (absorbing rounds that should have produced incapacitation), and a faster recovery curve from blunt trauma. Side-effect profile, inferred: probable cardiovascular strain, probable hepatic load, possible disinhibition of the already-present sadistic affect — observers note that post-enhancement his tactical patience subtly *worsens*, which is consistent with sub-cortical disinhibition.

**Episode B — Repeated cosmic-cube / Kobik-mediated re-shaping (Standoff / Pleasant Hill, Secret Empire).** Not pharmacological enhancement but reality-substrate editing. During Pleasant Hill he was rewritten into a non-violent civilian identity; the rewrite was not sustained and his original neural-behavioral configuration reasserted within hours of catalyzing exposure. The medically significant observation: **the rewrite was unstable in his case specifically.** Other subjects held longer. The most parsimonious reading is that his identity-organization around violence and the Skull-line is so deeply consolidated that even reality-engine substitution fails to overwrite it. This is a finding without precedent elsewhere in the file system; it argues for an unusually rigid, almost crystalline self-structure.

**Psychological impact of enhancement.** None of the *post-enhancement* introspective signatures one sees in other subjects — no anxiety about losing the enhancement, no addictive-seeking behavior to maintain it, no grandiose escalation of mission scope. He receives enhancement the way he receives any other tool issued by the Skull-line: he uses it while it is in his hand, and is unbothered when it leaves.

---

## M-6. THE DISFIGUREMENT EVENT — *Captain America: Reborn*

The single most consequential medical event of his life.

**Mechanism.** A short-range energy discharge from the Red Skull's then-host body during the Reborn-era sequence, focused on the face and scalp. Energy class: cosmic-cube–adjacent, not strictly thermal — meaning the burn pattern is anomalous and resistant to conventional reconstructive approaches.

**Acute pathology.** Full-thickness burns (DSM/burn-equivalent classification 3rd-degree with regions consistent with 4th-degree involvement) across the anterior face, scalp to the vertex, bilateral ear involvement, partial neck. Loss of nasal cartilage architecture. Loss of lip vermilion definition. Eyebrow loss, complete. Hair loss, complete and permanent across affected zones. Eyelid scarring with probable ongoing ectropion risk. Conjunctival irritation, chronic. Likely partial loss of corneal sensitivity in one or both eyes, producing the slow, unblinking quality his subordinates have learned to read as menace but which is, in part, an organic consequence of denervation.

**Subacute and chronic pathology.** Hypertrophic and contracture scarring across the mask zone, restricting facial expression — he can no longer smile in the muscular sense; what reads as a smile after disfigurement is the asymmetric retraction of scarred tissue. **Chronic neuropathic pain** across the burned regions, almost certainly continuous, almost certainly untreated by any sustained analgesic regimen (consistent with both Hydra-medical limitations and his own refusal to be pharmacologically dulled). Probable temperature-regulation dysfunction across the scalp; he runs cooler at the head than at the trunk, which the mask partly compensates. Olfactory function reduced, possibly absent — relevant operationally, as it removes one channel of environmental awareness he must consciously work around.

**Reconstructive approach.** None of consequence. Hydra surgical resources existed; he declined or was not offered sustained reconstruction. The mask was issued in its place — a tactical/symbolic prosthetic, not a medical one. This is the diagnostic moment: a patient with this injury who refuses reconstruction is communicating something. In Rumlow's case, the communication is not shame and not aesthetic resignation; it is a *recognition that the new face is more useful than the old.*

**Psychological impact — and the great anomaly.** A normative response to disfigurement of this magnitude includes acute depressive features, body-image disturbance, social withdrawal, suicidality risk, identity rupture, and, in many cases, persistent post-traumatic symptomatology. Rumlow exhibits **none of these.** Operational tempo *increases* post-injury. Aggression channeling becomes more efficient, not less. The mask is adopted not with reluctance but with what observers describe as a near-relief. The likeliest explanation: his pre-injury identity was already organized around being feared, and the injury removes the last residual obligation to negotiate a human face in human company. The disfigurement does not threaten his self; it ratifies it. From a clinical standpoint this is diagnostic of the underlying personality structure as much as any conduct in the record — a normal psyche cannot absorb a destroyed face this cleanly. His did because there was no countervailing self-image to defend.

**Latent vulnerability.** The one psychological exposure created by the injury is not the injury itself but its *visibility to the wrong audience*. Unmasking before the Skull-line, before Sin, before subordinates whose fear he requires, would activate a humiliation response his defenses are not built to absorb — his defenses are all outward-projecting. Unmasking before enemies, by contrast, would not wound him; enemies cannot diminish him.

---

## M-7. SUBSTANCE PROFILE

**Alcohol.** Light to moderate, situational, social-lubricant rather than self-medicative. He has been observed drinking in Hydra and mercenary social settings; there is no evidence of binge pattern, no evidence of withdrawal phenomena across captivity periods. He does not anesthetize.

**Tobacco.** Intermittent cigar use in down-time, possibly more for set-piece atmospherics than addiction; no chronic-smoker indicators in voice or skin pre-disfigurement.

**Recreational narcotics.** None evident. The mercenary subculture around him provides ample access; his abstinence is selective and deliberate.

**Performance-enhancing compounds.** Routine. Standard operator-tier stimulant use before high-tempo operations (consistent with caffeine and possibly modafinil-class agents), the Skull-supplied serum derivatives noted above, and almost certainly anabolic support across his thirties — though his hypertrophy pattern is more consistent with disciplined heavy-loading than with high-dose AAS.

**Analgesics.** **Notably under-utilized.** Post-disfigurement neuropathic pain would justify chronic opioid or anticonvulsant therapy; there is no evidence he accepts either. This is consistent with the personality finding: pharmacological dulling threatens the tactical-vigilance signature he has organized his entire adult life around.

**Psychiatric medications.** None, ever.

**Clinical interpretation of the substance profile.** The subject's substance pattern is in fact one of the strongest pieces of evidence *against* a primary mood, anxiety, or trauma diagnosis. People in chronic pain self-medicate. People with intrusive trauma phenomena self-medicate. People with affective dysregulation self-medicate. Rumlow does not. The absence is the data.

---

## M-8. SEXUAL AND REPRODUCTIVE HEALTH

Sexually active across the adult record. Coercive history beginning in adolescence (Savage Crims sexual assault). The Diamondback captivity sequence is sexually coded throughout — captivity, possession, the framing of forced proximity as courtship. Adult partnered relationship with Sin in the Brubaker-and-after period: apparently mutual, but the pair's shared reinforcement schedule pairs sexual and violent stimuli to a degree that, in any other patient population, would be flagged as paraphilic specifier. There is no documented offspring. No documented STI history, which in a man with this risk profile is a statistical anomaly best explained either by record-gap or by aggressive operator-medicine prophylaxis. Reproductive intent: absent — he shows no evidence of wanting progeny, no evidence of a generational-legacy fantasy. His legacy fantasy is *service*, not lineage.

**Post-disfigurement sexual functioning.** No evidence of degradation. Sin's continued partnership through and beyond the disfigurement is the strongest available data point: she does not appear to experience him as diminished, and he does not appear to experience himself as diminished in her presence. This further supports the M-6 finding that the injury did not destabilize his core self.

---

## M-9. MORTALITY EVENTS AND THE PATTERN OF RETURN

The record contains multiple events that should have been terminal — high-grade ballistic engagements, blast exposures, the Lagos detonation in the cinematic-adjacent peripheral material, recurrent "killed in action" reports across the comics continuity. He returns from each. The returns are sometimes explained by enhancement, sometimes by reality-substrate manipulation (Kobik), sometimes by the unreliability of the after-action report.

The behaviorally relevant fact is not that he survives — many of his peers survive — but that he survives **without** the recalibration that near-death usually imposes. Other operators emerge from near-death with revised threat models, narrowed risk appetite, occasional spiritual reframing. Rumlow emerges with his operational profile unchanged. He does not appear to register near-death as instructive. The most parsimonious clinical explanation is that he does not experience his own death as a meaningful category against which to update behavior — a finding consistent with the broader profile of an identity so fused to the Skull-line's mission that personal survival is a secondary parameter.

---

## M-10. SYNTHESIS — THE BODY AS DOCUMENT

The medical record of Brock Rumlow reads, taken whole, as the chart of a man who has used a body very hard for a very long time, refused most of the care that body required, and absorbed an injury that should have rewritten his identity without rewriting it at all. The somatic findings — the joint wear, the cumulative ballistic load, the burn pattern, the chronic untreated pain — describe a high-mileage instrument maintained at the minimum required for continued function. The *absences* — no substance-use pattern, no medication regimen, no avoidance of stimuli associated with prior trauma, no body-image disturbance after catastrophic disfigurement — are louder than the presences. They describe a psyche that does not use the body as a site of distress-expression because the distress is not there to express.

The single medical fact most worth preserving at the top of any future operational file: **the disfigurement did not break him because there was nothing in him that the disfigurement could break.** Treatment plans, redemption arcs, or interrogation strategies premised on the wounded face as a wedge will fail. The face is, to him, a more honest face than the one he was born with.

— END SECTION M. File continues at section P (Psychological — Longitudinal).


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: BROCK RUMLOW

*Compiled from longitudinal observation reconstruction. The body is the most honest document the subject keeps; he has been an operator long enough that his deliberate signatures are themselves data, and the involuntary signatures beneath them are data of a different kind. What follows is the file the body would write if it could be deposed.*

---

## 1. FRAME, MASS, AND THE BASELINE STANDING BODY

Subject stands approximately six foot one, weighs in the range of two-twenty to two-forty depending on operational cycle, and carries his mass forward of his heels — the weight distribution of a man whose default posture anticipates striking, not running. Shoulder girdle is dense, thickened from decades of pressing and rotational pulling work; trapezius hypertrophy reads visibly at the neck-line even under garments and creates the characteristic *short-necked* silhouette that registers, across the record, as bullish. Pelvis is held in slight anterior tilt, lumbar lordosis exaggerated by chronic posterior-chain loading; he does not stand fully *erect* so much as *coiled erect*, the knees never quite locked, a microflexion held continuously that most observers will not see but that fighters will recognize within seconds.

Arms hang slightly abducted from the torso at rest — the lat-driven "wide" stance of a man whose latissimus development has outpaced his hip mobility. Hands are habitually loose, fingers slightly curled, never in pockets. The pockets datum is consistent across every era of observation: he does not pocket his hands, ever, even in cold-weather civilian cover. Hands stay free.

Resting standing weight favors the right leg by a measurable margin, with the left held forward by perhaps five to ten degrees of foot angle — a *bladed* base he never quite drops. He does not stand square unless he is being still on purpose, which is itself a tell: square stance from him is a deliberate signal of non-threat, almost always tactical theater.

## 2. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

Walk is short-strided for his height, with a heel-to-toe contact that is heavier on the lateral edge of the foot than centerline — consistent with a long-term lifter's gait and with chronic mild lateral ankle instability from old injuries. The arm swing is *suppressed*: the right arm in particular barely crosses the midline, the elbow staying near the ribs in a permanent half-guard. Most civilians swing their arms to forty or fifty degrees of flexion in cadence; he runs closer to fifteen. The body never opens its centerline involuntarily.

Cadence shifts diagnostically by state. *At baseline*, walking pace is unhurried, almost ambling, and he covers ground slower than his peers; this is conscious — he wants the room scanned before he is in it. *Under approach to a target*, cadence accelerates only marginally but stride lengthens and the head stops moving laterally, fixing forward; this is the most reliable single pre-violence indicator he produces. *Under threat or pursuit*, he does not sprint as a first response; he transitions to a long, low, rolling jog that keeps his hands free and his head stable, the gait of a man trained to shoot while moving. Pure sprinting appears only when he has decided fighting is not the answer, which is rare enough that its presence in any incident report should be flagged as exceptional.

Stair behavior: ascends two at a time when alone, single-step when in formation; descends always single-step and always with the dominant hand near the trailing hip, where most of his concealed weaponry rides. Doorways: he *checks frames* habitually, a half-beat pause at any threshold during which his eyes finish the room before his body finishes the step. This is so automatic that he does it walking into his own quarters.

## 3. THE HANDS

The single most expressive part of his body, and the part he is least aware he is broadcasting through.

Knuckles are thickened — second and third metacarpals on both hands show the squared, calloused profile of long bare-knuckle and bag work; the calluses are *maintained*, not just acquired, indicating he still trains conditioning regularly in adulthood. Skin on the palms is dry, professionally maintained (a sweaty palm fails a trigger), nails kept short and squared. There is a healed laceration scar that runs across the web of the left thumb, consistent with a knife-defense slip; another shorter scar across the right index finger's proximal phalanx, consistent with a slide-bite from a sub-gauge pistol fired left-handed under stress (notable because it suggests he has, at least once, fired off-hand under conditions imperfect enough to draw blood and not corrected his grip in time).

*Gestural inventory.* He does not gesture conversationally in the Mediterranean sense — his hands rarely leave waist height while speaking. The gestures he does produce are small, downward, and chopping: a flat hand cut in front of the sternum when issuing a command, a knuckle tap on the nearest hard surface when impatient, a single index point that lands not at the listener but slightly past their ear, the shooter's habit of designating a target *through* the human rather than at them. When listening to a superior — historically the Skull, latterly Sin — the hands clasp loosely in front of the belt, a posture borrowed from the parade-rest of military service but held lower and closer to the body, a tell of subordination he produces for no one else.

*Stress migration of hand position.* Calm: hands open, loose, hanging. Mildly irritated: right thumb rubs the pad of the right index finger in a slow circular motion, sometimes for minutes at a time — the most reliable low-level discomfort signal he produces. Pre-violence: the rubbing stops, the right hand drops to mid-thigh height, fingers go from curled to extended-and-still. Active threat: both hands rise simultaneously to between waist and sternum, palms inward, fingers slightly curled — *the cage*, his standing guard, which he assumes without conscious decision. Post-engagement, win: hands flex and re-flex several times, slow, almost luxurious; he is unloading adrenaline through the smaller musculature, and he does not hide it because around his own people he sees no reason to. Post-engagement, loss or aborted contact: hands go *still*, unnaturally so, and stay still until he is alone — the deliberate suppression of any tell that would read as agitation.

## 4. HEAD, NECK, AND THE EYE-LINE

Head carriage is forward of the shoulders by perhaps half an inch — the chin-down, brow-forward set of a man who has spent decades looking through a scope, through a faceplate, or through opponents. Neck rotates more than most observers expect for the mass at the shoulders; he keeps cervical mobility deliberately because his peripheral vision is his primary survival sense. The head moves on a *slow horizontal scan* at rest, traversing the visual field on a cycle of roughly six to ten seconds, never jerky, never twitchy — a learned discipline that suppresses the orienting reflex of normal civilian attention.

*Eye behavior.* Gaze is steady, unhurried, and *low-blink* — blink rate runs measurably below average, particularly when assessing a person; he stares without intending to. In conversation he does not maintain the polite alternating gaze of social norms; he locks on, then *releases* deliberately to scan, then re-locks. Pupils dilate readily under stimulus but recover quickly, an autonomic signature consistent with the unusually stable affect regulation noted in the psychological profile. He does not look at people's eyes when threatening them — he looks at their throats, sternum, or hands, the targeting triangle, and the victims who survive him often remember this specifically: that he stopped seeing them as a person at a definable moment.

Pre-disfigurement, the resting facial expression was a low-grade asymmetric smirk, the right corner of the mouth carried fractionally higher than the left, brow neutral — the contemptuous default of a man amused by what he is watching. Post-disfigurement, with the mask habitually worn, the *visible* face is the mask; underneath, where it can be observed at all (medical examination, intimate settings, the rare unmasked operational moment), scar contracture has pulled the right side of the mouth and lower eyelid into a fixed pull-down, producing an involuntary snarl-set even at rest. He has not corrected for this. He may prefer it.

Jaw clenches as the primary visible cranial tell. Masseter hypertrophy is pronounced; he grinds bilaterally in sleep (almost certainly, given the wear pattern that would be evident on dentition), and clenches awake under cognitive load. The single most reliable readable-through-the-mask emotion is anger, because the masseters move the cheekbones of the mask itself.

## 5. THE MASK — WEAR PATTERN AND DOFFING RITUAL

The skull-faced tactical mask is not a costume piece; treat it as an integrated prosthetic. He puts it on in a fixed sequence: lower jaw cup first, then the cranial shell down over the brow, then the rear retention strap, then a single press-test of both temples with the heels of his hands to confirm seat. He does this with eyes closed for the strap step, every time — a ritual stability cue, the only consistent self-soothing micro-behavior in his entire somatic inventory.

He removes the mask in private with a sequence that is the inverse but slower: rear strap, cranial shell lifted off straight upward (never tilted, which would scrape the burn scarring), jaw cup last. The first thing he does with the bare face is *exhale*, long and audible, through the nose — the pressure-equalization breath of a diver surfacing. Then a single touch of the right hand to the lower right cheek, fingertips only, brief, almost checking that the face is still there. He does not look at his face in mirrors; mirrors in his quarters are positioned for over-shoulder threat-check, not self-inspection.

In the mask, his vocal resonance shifts lower and more chest-driven (the cup damps higher frequencies), and his breathing becomes audible to anyone within a meter — a fact he uses deliberately, slowing the breath to make the audibility itself a threat signal.

## 6. VOICE, BREATH, AND SOUND-MAKING

Voice is a low baritone with a New York Lower East Side substrate that he has never sanded off — the vowel placements still register, particularly the flattened *a* and the dropped post-vocalic *r* under stress, even when his speech is otherwise neutral. He speaks at lower volume than his size would predict; he has learned that quiet from him reads more dangerous than loud. Pace is *slow*, with characteristic mid-sentence pauses that are not searching for words — he knows the words — but are deliberately compelling the listener to lean in. This is the *terror-craftsman* speech pattern: every sentence engineered to make the listener wait for it.

He laughs rarely, and when he does it is a short, low, three- or four-beat exhalation through the nose, almost soundless, accompanied by a barely-perceptible shoulder shake. Laughter is almost always at someone's expense — a victim's fear, a subordinate's mistake, an enemy's miscalculation. Genuine surprise, by contrast, produces a single huffed *hah*, equally short, but accompanied by a head tilt that the snickering version does not include.

*Breathing patterns by state.* Resting respiration is slow, diaphragmatic, nasal-dominant — perhaps ten to twelve breaths per minute, well below the civilian average. Under combat load, he breathes through tactical patterns (likely box-breathing or a similar four-count discipline acquired in training); the breath becomes shallower but never panicked, and the recovery between bursts is exceptionally fast, consistent with his lifetime conditioning. The only state in which his breath audibly changes in a way he does not control is *rage* — specifically rage triggered by insult to the Skull-line — at which point the nostrils flare visibly on the inhalation, the exhalation goes audible and through the teeth, and the cadence becomes irregular. This is the body of a man whose self-regulation is, as the psychological profile noted, *borrowed* from the cause; when the cause is touched, the borrowed regulation fails.

Coughing, sneezing, throat-clearing — all suppressed to near-zero in operational settings, executed normally only when alone. He has trained his body not to broadcast.

## 7. GROOMING, DRESS, AND OBJECT-RELATION TO THE BODY

Hair is kept short, military-cropped, with no detectable variation across decades — he does not experiment with his appearance and has not since adolescence. He shaves daily when un-masked life requires it; the shaving is fast, no ceremony, against the grain on a face that no longer has full sensation in places. Body hair on the torso is dense and uncultivated; he does not depilate or shape.

Clothing is utilitarian and *fitted* — never loose enough to snag on a draw, never tight enough to restrict the shoulder. The covert-civilian wardrobe runs to dark tactical trousers, low boots, dark long-sleeve shirts, jackets cut for concealed carry; he owns essentially no clothing he could not fight in. He does not wear watches on the wrist (interferes with sleeves and wrist locks), preferring pocket-clipped timepieces or vehicle/HUD time. He does not wear rings, chains, or other jewelry — no purchase points for a grappler.

Boots are *broken in and replaced on a cycle* rather than allowed to wear out; the soles are checked routinely. He laces double-knotted with the bow tucked under the upper lace — a paratrooper's lacing — and the lacing is identical on both boots to the millimeter. Small obsessions like this are not generalized OCD-spectrum behavior; they are domain-specific to gear, and they reveal where his actual care lives.

The tactical kit, when worn, is positioned with the same compulsive uniformity. Magazine pouches at consistent indexed positions, blade at a consistent draw, sidearm at a consistent ride height. He does not improvise loadout. He resents subordinates who do.

## 8. SLEEP

Sleep is short, efficient, and *positional*. He sleeps on his back or right side, never face-down (face-down compromises the draw from a bedside weapon). Total sleep duration averages four to six hours in operational periods and stretches to seven only in extended downtime, which he tolerates poorly. He sleeps with a weapon within arm's reach, always on the dominant side — not under the pillow, which is a movie habit, but on a hard surface where it will not be displaced by sleep movement.

Sleep onset is fast, characteristic of high-functioning operators — under five minutes from horizontal to unconsciousness in most conditions. Sleep is interrupted easily by auditory anomaly and almost not at all by visual change; he wakes by hearing. Wake transition is *immediate and oriented*: from sleep to weapon-in-hand in well under two seconds, no grogginess phase, no disorientation window. This is trained but also temperamental — he does not have the slow surfacing of a man whose unconscious holds him.

Dreaming is unknown to the file, but the absence of any documented intrusion phenomena, nightmares, or sleep-disturbance complaints across the record is itself diagnostically consistent with the no-PTSD finding. He sleeps the sleep of a man who has done many things and is bothered by none of them.

He does not nap socially — he naps *strategically*, fifteen to twenty minutes at a time, in vehicles, in transit, in pre-mission staging, and rises from these with the same instant orientation.

## 9. EATING AND ORAL BEHAVIOR

Eats functionally, large quantities, on a fixed daily caloric throughput consistent with maintaining his mass through chronic training load. Preferences run to protein-dense, simple-carbohydrate, low-variety food — the eating pattern of a man who treats meals as fueling events. He eats *fast* but not sloppily; clean utensil use, minimal table conversation, eyes up during chewing. He does not drink heavily — beer or modest spirits, almost never to intoxication, because intoxication compromises the apparatus he has spent his life building. He drinks water in large volumes between meals.

He does not smoke as a primary habit but will accept a cigarette socially — a transactional gesture more than a craving, which puts him in the unusual category of operator who reads as a smoker and isn't. Coffee intake is substantial, black, no ceremony around it.

Oral self-stimulation behaviors: a slow, lateral tongue-press against the inside of the right cheek when thinking, sometimes paired with the jaw-clench; occasional teeth-suck (the soft *tsk* drawn inward) when displeased with a subordinate, which has become a recognizable warning to those who work under him. He does not chew gum, does not chew toothpicks, does not chew the inside of his lip — the oral fixations stay tongue-and-teeth, never habits that would change his face shape mid-engagement.

## 10. PAIN, INJURY, AND SOMATIC SUPPRESSION

He under-displays pain to a clinically remarkable degree. Gunshot wounds taken in combat have, in the record, produced a momentary positional adjustment and continued engagement; he does not vocalize on impact, does not clutch wounds for show, does not sit down. This is partly trained, partly temperamental, and partly — given the chronic neuropathic load from the burn injuries — habituation: the man's baseline pain experience is higher than most healthy adults' acute pain ceiling, so additional pain registers as gradient, not event.

Chronic-pain micro-behaviors that *do* leak: a slow rotation of the right shoulder mid-conversation (old injury, almost certainly rotator cuff residual); intermittent flexion-extension of the right hand fingers held below table line (carpal-tunnel or cumulative metacarpal strain); occasional weight-shifts off the left hip when standing for extended periods (probable healed pelvic or femoral insult). He will not acknowledge any of these if asked. They are involuntary, and they are diagnostic.

He does not take analgesics in any documented pattern. The personality-congruent denial of pain noted in the psychiatric workup expresses itself somatically as a refusal to medicate; the pain is part of the apparatus, not an interruption of it.

## 11. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE SOMATICS

The intimate body is the same body as the operational body, with the same dominance gradient, the same possession-coded reach, the same suppression of vulnerability cues. Touch initiated by him is *acquisitive* — palm-down on the back of the neck, fingers spread on the small of the back with thumb hooked at the spine, hand cupped under the jaw with thumb at the chin — gestures that orient the partner's body rather than meeting it. He does not initiate touch in the *receiving* sense; he is not held, and on the rare occasions when a partner has attempted to hold him in any tender register, the body goes still and the breath shallows in a way that reads — even to him — as withdrawal.

With Sin specifically, the somatic register shifts in a measurable way. Touch becomes less acquisitive and more *parallel* — shoulder to shoulder, hip to hip, the two bodies oriented at the same target rather than at each other. This is closer to comradeship than romance in its body language, and is the only documented intimate relationship in which he displays anything resembling lateral attachment. The eroticism between them, where it surfaces, is paired with shared violence — proximate combat appears to function as foreplay in this dyad, and the post-combat physical contact is more affectionate than the pre-combat physical contact.

With Diamondback, historically, the touch was *captor-touch* throughout — restraint coded as intimacy, proximity as possession. He does not appear to know the difference, somatically, and the file should record this not as a misunderstanding but as a *capacity absence*. The relational dialect simply does not contain the word for non-coercive touch.

The face in genuine arousal (rare and largely pre-disfigurement records): the smirk widens, the eye-blink rate further suppresses, the breath audibly deepens. Post-disfigurement intimate observation is sparse; the mask is removed for sex with intimates only.

## 12. STATE-DEPENDENT POSTURAL ATLAS — A QUICK REFERENCE

*Calm / baseline:* bladed stance, right leg loaded, hands loose, head slow-scanning, jaw soft, breath nasal and slow, voice low and unhurried. The smirk, where the face is visible.

*Cognitive load / planning:* weight distribution evens, tongue moves to right cheek, right thumb circles right index pad, gaze defocuses to middle distance for short intervals, breath unchanged.

*Mild irritation:* the thumb-pad rub intensifies; teeth-suck appears; voice drops further in volume rather than rising; pace of speech *slows*. The slow voice is the warning.

*Pre-violence intent:* thumb-rub stops abruptly; right hand drops to mid-thigh; head-scanning stops, gaze locks forward; bladed stance deepens; jaw clenches visibly; breath shifts to four-count discipline. Voice frequently goes silent here — the loquaciousness of the cruelty-craftsman is reserved for *during* and *after* the engagement, not before.

*Active engagement:* the cage guard rises; cadence and stride elongate; breath is patterned; verbalization, if any, is short, declarative, often taunting. Sadistic verbal content peaks during, not before — he is feeding on the victim's recognition in real time.

*Post-engagement, victorious:* hands flex-and-release repeatedly; shoulders drop perceptibly; the laugh, if it appears, appears here; a slow exhale through the nose; the body unwinds in a sequence that runs shoulders, neck, jaw, hands — top-down.

*Post-engagement, failed or aborted:* the body locks. Hands still, face still, gaze fixed. Silence. This state is the most dangerous state he produces, because the suppression must vent somewhere, and historically it vents on whoever is next in proximity.

*Rage triggered by insult to the Skull-line:* nostrils flare, exhale audibly through the teeth, the head drops *forward* slightly (a bull-set), shoulders rise toward the ears (rare for him — he normally holds them low), and tactical patience collapses. The body forgets its discipline. This is the only state in which he becomes predictable, and it is the only state in which he can be beaten by an opponent he should not lose to.

*Devotion / submission to a superior in the Skull-line:* the parade-rest hand clasp at the belt; chin lifts marginally to expose the throat in a way he exposes it to no one else; voice rises in pitch by a measurable interval; weight evens between both feet, square stance. This is the *only* configuration in his somatic repertoire that resembles a child's posture before a parent, and its presence in any encounter is a flag of the relational geometry he is operating inside.

*Intimacy, non-coercive (rare):* breath shallows; body stills; the absence of acquisitive touch initiation; a faintly observable holding-of-self that suggests the state is being tolerated rather than entered. The body does not know how to receive; the file should record this as a permanent feature, not a phase.

---

## CLOSING NOTE TO FILE

The somatic record converges with the psychological: this is a body that has been *organized* around a purpose, not interrupted by one. The tells are operational, not neurotic. The micro-behaviors that leak around the discipline — the thumb-rub, the teeth-suck, the shoulder roll, the strap-press with closed eyes, the long nasal exhale after the mask comes off — are the only


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS — SUBJECT: BROCK RUMLOW

## I. The Developmental Substrate: An Attachment Vacuum

The file contains, conspicuously, no parents. No mother named, no father invoked even in rage or contempt, no siblings, no aunt, no priest, no teacher, no first girl, no childhood friend who later turned up dead or straight. This absence is itself the datum. Across thirty-five years of published material — including stretches written by authors (Brubaker, Remender, Spencer) who routinely furnish their villains with parental flashbacks as connective tissue — Rumlow has never been given one. The omission is too durable to be accidental; it is structural. The character is rendered, consistently, as a man who arrives on the page already formed by the street.

What this means in attachment terms: there is no evidence of a primary caregiver figure who provided a secure base, and equally no evidence of a *named* abuser. The likely developmental picture, reconstructed from the conduct that follows, is one of profound early **neglect** rather than focal early **trauma**. A focally traumatized child tends to organize around the trauma — re-enacts it, avoids it, dissociates around it. Rumlow does none of these things. What he displays instead is the signature of a child raised, effectively, by the ambient environment: the building, the block, the older boys, the rules of the corner. The Lower East Side of the late 1960s and 1970s, as he would have known it, was the parent. The Savage Crims were the family of origin in any functional sense.

This produces what is, in adult presentation, a **disorganized-then-coercive** attachment profile. The disorganized component — the absence of a coherent template for "trusted other" — is filled, in adolescence, by a coercive template imported from the gang: relating *is* dominance hierarchy. The Crims did not teach him that love and violence were opposites; they taught him they were the same instrument used in different directions. Care meant having someone above you who would punish enemies on your behalf. Loyalty meant the kind of fear that doesn't run. Sex was a use of bodies. Betrayal was a tactical event, not a moral one. This is the ground floor of every relationship he will ever have.

## II. The Architecture of Verticality

Rumlow's relational world is **strictly vertical**. There is no documented friendship in the entire record — no peer he confides in, no equal he drinks with off-duty, no man his own age and rank he treats as a brother. Every relationship he sustains is plotted on a single up-down axis, and the axis is not negotiable.

**Upward bonds (devotional).** To the Red Skull, and through the Skull to the Skull-line: Sin as inheritor, Skadi as the Skull-line in mythic form, the Hydra-Cap incarnation of Steve Rogers as the Skull-line's prophesied culmination. These bonds are characterized by:

- *Unconditional service.* He does not bargain over assignments. He does not flinch at the suicide-coded ones. When the Skull orders something humiliating or strategically wasteful of him, he performs it without renegotiation. This is not because he lacks tactical judgment — he often has better tactical judgment than the order reflects — but because the *bond is the point*; obedience is the relationship's medium.
- *Identification, not affection.* He does not appear to *like* the Skull in any ordinary sense. He does not seek the Skull's company for its own sake, does not engage in social grooming, does not joke with him. The relationship is closer to that of a knight to a sacred king: the king's person is the axis of the world, but one does not become *close* to the king. One stations oneself.
- *Invariance under substitution.* The most diagnostic feature. When the Skull is dead, he serves the Skull's body inside Lukin. When the Skull's daughter takes up the hammer, he serves her as Skadi. When Steve Rogers is the Skull's project (Hydra-Cap), he serves Rogers. The *person* of the Skull is not what he is attached to; the **Skull-function** is. He has bonded to a *role* and pursues whoever currently occupies it. This is theologically structured attachment — closer to the way a worshipper relates to a deity who may take many incarnations than to the way a man loves another man.

**Downward bonds (commanding).** To strike-team subordinates, to the lower tiers of Skull's apparatus, to henchmen pulled in for specific operations. These are characterized by:

- *Brutal competence demand.* He will tolerate sadism, idiocy, ugliness, ideological hash in a subordinate. He will not tolerate inability. Operators who underperform are killed or discarded with no observable affective residue.
- *Cultivated terror.* He runs teams on fear. The mask, the voice, the unpredictability of his moods, the public discipline of failures — all are deliberate. He grasps that a team that fears its commander outperforms one that likes him, and he has no use for being liked.
- *Mentorial fragment.* Residue from his time as Taskmaster's senior instructor: he can teach, and occasionally does, and when he does it is technically excellent. But the teaching is never paired with affection; he transmits skill the way a smith transmits forging — the apprentice is grateful and afraid, not loved.

**Lateral bonds: structurally absent.** This is the most striking feature of the entire record. In a profession dense with peer relationships — mercenary culture is famously, almost compulsively, fraternal — Rumlow does not have one. He has worked alongside Batroc, the Wrecking Crew, various Hydra operatives, the entire field roster of the Skull's organization, and there is no evidence in canon that he considers any of them a friend, a confidant, or even a regular drinking partner. The closest approach is **Sin**, and Sin is not a peer; Sin is the Skull-line. He has had decades to form a fraternal bond with someone and has never done so. This is not coincidence; it is a structural inability. Lateral relating requires that the other be neither above nor below — a category his nervous system does not recognize.

## III. Sin: The Apparent Exception That Confirms the Rule

The bond with Sinthea Schmidt is the single relationship in the record that *looks* like a partnership. They run hit teams together, fight side by side, are sexually involved across long arcs, and when she becomes Skadi he serves her with the same devotion he gave her father. To a casual reader this might present as the one peer attachment of his life.

It is not. The structure is more interesting and more revealing.

Sin sits at the intersection of every one of his attachment vectors simultaneously: she is *upward* (she is Skull-line, and after the Skull's death she is the Skull-line's living embodiment); she is *downward* (in early years she was the younger, smaller operator he occasionally guided through tradecraft); and she is *possessable* (woman, sexual partner, frequently in scenes where the framing has him as the more physically formidable). She is the only person in his world who fits all three of his available relational gears at once, and so the bond with her presents an unusual *density* — but each individual strand of it is one of his standard moves, not a novel form of relating.

The diagnostic test is what happens when these vectors come into tension. When Sin is endangered, his upward-devotional response dominates: he abandons mission discipline, becomes tactically rash, will burn assets to reach her. When she is dominant (Skadi, hammer in hand), he subordinates seamlessly. When she is wounded and dependent, the possessive register comes forward. He does not *negotiate* between these modes; he switches between them as her presentation dictates. Sin functions as his most complete object precisely because she is *plural* in the ways his attachment apparatus needs.

What is absent, even with her: any evidence that he confides in her about his interior, that he seeks her opinion on matters outside their shared operational and ideological field, that he is curious about her as a separate consciousness. They share a project and a bed; they do not, as far as the record shows, share a self.

## IV. Diamondback: The Unfinished Possession

The Rachel Leighton arc is the most extensively documented intimate behavior in Rumlow's file and consequently the most diagnostically useful. He kidnaps her after her defection from the Serpent Society to Cap's orbit. He tortures her — and the torture is explicitly framed by him as a courtship modality. He tells her he loves her while inflicting pain. He keeps her. When she escapes, he hunts her. When she has moved on, he experiences this not as loss but as *theft*: she is something of his that someone else now possesses.

Several features warrant granular note:

- **The use of romantic vocabulary.** He does not call what he wants from her "ownership"; he calls it love. This is not strategic dissimulation. The vocabulary appears in his internal narration as well as his speech. He has no other word for what he feels, because the affect *itself* is undifferentiated possession-and-arousal that the surrounding culture taught him to label love.
- **The absence of seduction.** He never, across the entire arc, attempts to *win* her. The script of pursuit-courtship-consent is wholly absent from his behavioral repertoire. He moves directly from notice to seizure. This is not a failure of romantic skill; it is the absence of the schema. He does not understand that consent is a thing one can pursue, because in his developmental world it was not.
- **The longevity of the grudge.** Years after the arc has nominally closed, mention of Diamondback still destabilizes him. This is the only person whose name produces in him an affective spike not mediated by the Skull-line. The hypothesis: she is the only target he has ever *failed* to possess, and the failure occupies a slot in his self-concept that nothing else can fill. Her existence is the empirical refutation of his omnicompetence in the one register he allows himself to want anything in.
- **What this rules out.** It rules out any reading of his relating to her as ordinary obsession, stalking, or romantic fixation in the civilian sense. It is closer to the affect a collector has toward the one piece that got away — except that the piece is a person and the collector is a torturer.

The Diamondback case is the cleanest demonstration in the file that Rumlow's intimacy gear is *coercive possession*, full stop. There is no second gear. When he wants someone, the wanting and the taking are the same motion.

## V. Steve Rogers: Hate as Negative Attachment

Across decades, Rumlow's most stable adversarial bond is with Steve Rogers. This relationship has the structural properties of an attachment even though its valence is hate.

He thinks about Rogers more than he thinks about most of the people who are nominally on his own side. He plans against him with care. He pulled the trigger himself on the Federal Courthouse steps when he could have had a subordinate do it — the kill was personally important. And later, when Steve Rogers becomes the Hydra-Cap incarnation of the Skull-line, the bond inverts seamlessly from hatred to devotion. The man does not change; Rumlow's read of the man's *function* changes, and his behavior follows.

The diagnostic content: Rumlow does not hate Rogers because Rogers opposes him operationally. He hates Rogers because Rogers represents the proposition that a man with great strength might choose *not* to use it for dominance. This proposition is, in Rumlow's worldview, an obscenity — an insult to the natural order in which strength is *for* dominance. Rogers is the standing demonstration that Rumlow's organizing premise is contestable, and the existence of the demonstration is intolerable. When Hydra-Cap appears to repudiate the demonstration, the obscenity is removed, and the figure who carried it becomes, instead, the awaited leader. The pivot is not opportunism; it is theological relief.

## VI. The Mask, the Face, and the Foreclosure of Intimacy

The disfigurement during the Reborn sequence has been catalogued in the medical file as physically severe with anomalously absent psychological sequelae. In the relational register, however, it has one major effect: it forecloses any residual possibility of intimate relating *outside* the operational frame.

Rumlow's face, post-burn, is something he cannot present to a stranger in a bar, a clerk at a counter, a woman across a restaurant table. The mask becomes obligatory for any continuous social functioning. This means that every interaction he has is now *staged* as an interaction with Crossbones, the symbol, rather than with Brock Rumlow, the man. There is no longer a register in which he could, even theoretically, meet someone as a civilian.

He does not appear to mourn this. The likeliest reading is that he had already foreclosed civilian intimacy decades earlier and the burn merely externalized the foreclosure. But it matters for the relational map because it explains why even Sin, even his closest subordinates, even his Hydra colleagues, encounter the mask far more often than the face. The number of people on Earth who have seen him unmasked since the injury and survived is small, and the act of unmasking before someone is, for him, a charged event whose meaning is *not* intimacy in the ordinary sense but a *granting of subordinate access* — closer to a king allowing a vassal to see him at prayer than to a lover allowing himself to be seen at rest.

## VII. Trust, Distrust, Betrayal

**Trust** in the conventional sense — believing the other will act with goodwill toward one's interests — is not a category Rumlow operates in. What he uses instead is **reliability assessment**: he calibrates, with professional accuracy, what a given other can be expected to do under specified incentives. He "trusts" Sin in the sense that he has high-confidence predictions of her behavior in the relevant ranges. He does not "trust" her in the sense of believing she would protect him at cost to herself if no incentive aligned, because that is not a question his cognitive frame poses.

**Distrust** is similarly atypical. He does not become suspicious of allies in the paranoid register; he simply maintains a continuous reliability estimate and adjusts. Subordinates who fail an estimate are removed. Equals — to the extent he encounters any — are assessed and dispatched as the situation warrants. The Skull-line is exempt from assessment; it is the axis on which the assessment apparatus rests, and so cannot itself be subjected to it. This is the most theologically interesting feature of his cognition: there is, structurally, an article of faith.

**Betrayal**, as something *he commits*, is frequent and unburdened by guilt. He has burned employers, allies, temporary partners, women, subordinates — whenever the Skull-line's project required it or his own survival within that project required it. The act produces no remorse and no narrative reframing; he does not need to tell himself a story about why the betrayal was justified, because his frame already designates whatever serves the Skull-line as justified by definition. This is what makes him operationally useful to the Skull: he carries no ballast.

**Betrayal as something *committed against him*** is harder to document because it has rarely happened in a form he recognizes. He has been outmaneuvered, captured, defeated — none of these register as betrayal because none of them violate a relational expectation he held. The closest the file comes to a genuine betrayal-of-Rumlow event is the various points at which the Skull has used him as bait, sacrificed him for larger plays, or simply forgotten about him. He absorbs these without protest. The most plausible interpretation: he does not experience them as betrayal because *he does not believe the Skull owes him anything*. Use is the relationship's content. To be used is to be in it.

The single registered exception — the only event-class that would, theoretically, register as betrayal — is hypothesized in the pressure-points analysis: a definitive demonstration that the Skull-line has *contempt* for him, has used him not as a valuable instrument but as a worthless one. This has never occurred in canon, and his response to it is therefore conjectural. The conjecture: identity collapse, because there is no alternative narrative to absorb the data.

## VIII. Repair: A Capacity Absent from the Repertoire

In healthy attachment, ruptures are followed by repair — apology, accountability, adjustment, the restoration of bond after offense.
