Rumlow's relational repertoire contains no observable repair behavior. When a bond is damaged, he does not initiate restoration; he either replaces the bond, eliminates the other party, or treats the rupture as the new equilibrium and proceeds.

This is consistent with the absence of guilt, the absence of remorse, the absence of affective empathy. Repair requires that the rupture be felt as a *loss* by the offending party, and the offending party then act to restore. Rumlow does not feel ruptures as losses. The relational economy he operates in does not contain the currency repair is paid in.

The corollary: he does not *expect* repair from others either. When a subordinate fails him, he does not entertain the possibility that the subordinate might atone; the failure is the verdict. When an ally proves unreliable, the ally is reclassified, not rehabilitated. This produces relationships of striking *crispness* — they work or they end, and the transition is fast and final.

## IX. Dependency

A man whose attachment world is organized around service to an authoritarian object is, by definition, profoundly dependent. The dependency is invisible to him because its object is so totalizing that it functions as the ambient atmosphere rather than as a perceived need. Fish do not perceive water; Rumlow does not perceive that the Skull-line is the precondition of his coherent functioning.

The dependency presents in several operational features:

- *Restlessness in the Skull's absence.* The periods when the Skull has been definitively dead and no successor has yet emerged are the periods of his greatest disorganization. He drifts, takes contracts of declining strategic interest, expresses an irritability his subordinates find more dangerous than his usual cruelty. He is, in the technical sense, *bereaved* — though he would never use the word and the affect does not present as grief, only as friction.
- *Speed of attachment to successors.* The transfer of devotion to Sin-as-Skadi, to the Hydra-Cap incarnation, occurs without an intervening period of reflection. The need to attach is so acute that successor-recognition is almost reflexive.
- *Inability to refuse mission.* Even when the mission is strategically poor, even when his own tactical judgment objects, he accepts. The cost of refusal — momentary independence from the Skull-line — is greater than any conceivable operational cost.

This dependency is also what bounds his autonomy. He has the skills to operate independently as a high-end mercenary, the intelligence to run his own enterprise, the discipline to sustain it. He has never done so for any length of time. The Pleasant Hill interlude, where he was psychically reconstituted as a civilian named Frank without the Skull-frame, is the only period in his adult life when he existed outside the Skull-line, and it was *imposed* — and dissolved on contact with his own memories.

## X. Intimacy

To the extent intimacy means *being known*, Rumlow is not intimate with anyone. He does not narrate his interior to others, does not ask others to narrate theirs to him, does not engage in the small mutual disclosures that constitute the texture of close relationship. Sin probably knows him as well as anyone alive, and the file gives little reason to think she knows him deeply. He does not have a confidant. He does not have, in the available evidence, *thoughts he tells*.

This is not a deficit he experiences as one. The interior he would have to disclose is not, by his own internal measure, *interesting* — it is operational, it is ideological, it is appetitive. He sees no reason to narrate it because it does not feel to him like a private treasury whose sharing is a gift. Intimacy as gift-economy is foreign to him.

To the extent intimacy means *bodily proximity and access*, he has had it — with Diamondback under coercion, with Sin under partnership. But the bodily intimacy is not coupled to disclosure. Sex for him is an act among other shared acts; it does not produce a category of "after," when partners speak in lower voices about what they have not said before. The file suggests the after, for Rumlow, looks much like the before.

## XI. The Relational Template, Stated Plainly

A single template repeats across every relationship in his life. Stated explicitly:

> *There is one above me whose project organizes the world; I serve it. There are those below me whom I move through fear toward the project's ends. There are enemies, whose terror and destruction is the project's content and my pleasure. There are objects of want — women, primarily — whom I take. There are no equals; the category does not exist.*

Every relational episode in the canon fits this template. The Skull, Sin-as-Skadi, Hydra-Cap occupy the upper slot serially. Strike teams, Crims, Hydra subordinates occupy the lower slot serially. Captain America, the Avengers, Bucky Barnes, the Punisher occupy the enemy slot. Diamondback, and others less documented, occupy the want slot. The slots are stable; the occupants vary.

What is striking about a life this long lived inside a template this narrow is not the narrowness — many violent men live inside narrow templates — but the **stability**. Most antisocial personalities of this severity burn through their templates: they exhaust the upward object through their own rebellion, they kill too many subordinates to keep a team, they cannot sustain the want-object beyond a kidnapping. Rumlow has sustained the same upper slot for forty published years across multiple incarnations of its occupant, has maintained operational capacity to recruit and command subordinates throughout, has maintained the want-object as a stable internal fixture even after losing access to its referent. He is, by the standards of his diagnostic class, *unusually durable*.

The durability is the Skull's gift to him. The relational architecture he brought from the Lower East Side would, left to itself, have produced a much shorter and more chaotic life. The encounter with the Red Skull supplied an object stable enough to hold the architecture across decades. This is the central, perverse truth of Brock Rumlow's relational existence: the most violent ideological movement of his century gave him the only sustained relational coherence he was ever going to have. He did not serve the Skull-line because he was broken into doing so. He served it because, in the structure of his psyche, it was the only object large enough to be served.

— END SECTION.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DOSSIER SECTION — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## Subject: Brock Rumlow / Crossbones
### Section Classification: Structural-Defensive Architecture, Longitudinal

---

## 0. Orienting Frame

Most subjects accumulate a defensive system in layers — a neurotic upper crust (humor, sublimation, intellectualization) sitting atop an immature middle (projection, acting-out, somatization) sitting atop a primitive floor (splitting, denial, identification with the aggressor). The clinician's job is usually to read down through the layers.

Rumlow does not have layers. He has a **floor**, and on the floor he has built a **prosthesis** — a curated public self (Crossbones, the mask, the voice, the silhouette) that performs the function ego-defenses normally perform internally. He has **externalized** his defenses into a persona and a uniform. This is the structural fact that organizes everything below.

He does not need to repress, sublimate, or reframe because he does not experience the affects those defenses would manage. The threat that ordinary defenses metabolize — shame, guilt, fear of annihilation, fear of insignificance — is, in Rumlow, handled by ensuring that the *world* contains those affects in others, on demand, generated by him. He doesn't process the feelings; he *donates* them.

What follows is the full inventory.

---

## 1. The Primitive Floor — Ranked by Centrality

### 1.1 Identification with the Aggressor *(load-bearing defense)*

This is the keystone of the structure. Every other defense rests on it.

**Mechanism in this subject.** The classical Ferenczi-Anna Freud formulation — child internalizes the threatening adult to neutralize fear by becoming the source of fear — operates in Rumlow without the developmental friction that usually limits it. There is no documented protective adult to contest the identification; the Savage Crims peer ecology rewarded it; the Red Skull capitalized it. By adulthood the defense is not a defense in the active sense at all — it has consolidated into character. He *is* the aggressor; there is no residual identifying-with going on. The verb has become the noun.

**Behavioral signature.** Cultivation of a name that is a mode of death (Crossbones). Cultivation of a face that is a death's-head (the mask, retained after disfigurement even when restoration to a human face would have been possible during the Pleasant Hill restoration). Vocal register pitched low and slow in operational contexts — observed across writers, the deliberate underplaying of menace that is more frightening than shouting. Body management: the deliberate stillness when others would fidget, the calibrated approach-walk to a restrained captive. Every micro-behavior is the same macro-defense iterated downward.

**Tell.** When the defense is functioning he is calm. When the defense is *thwarted* — when an enemy refuses to be afraid of him, when a victim laughs, when a peer treats him as ordinary muscle — the underlying structure is briefly visible as rage. Cap, more than any other adversary, produces this thwarting reliably, because Rogers will not perform the fear Rumlow needs him to perform. This is the deepest reason Rumlow hates him.

### 1.2 Splitting

**Mechanism.** Persons and entities sort cleanly into two bins, with no observed capacity for integration. Skull-line / not-Skull-line. Strong / weak. Owned / unowned. Useful / disposable. There is no documented instance, across the canon, of Rumlow holding ambivalent feeling about a person — no "I respect him but disagree," no "she wronged me but I understand why." The closest the record comes is Diamondback, and even there the ambivalence is not held internally; it is *acted out* as alternating capture-and-punishment, which is splitting externalized into behavior.

**Behavioral signature.** Targeting decisions are categorical. Once an enemy is designated, no information modifies the designation. This is operationally an asset (no hesitation, no second-guessing) and a liability (no updating when the target's role changes). His treatment of subordinates is similarly bimodal: in or out, with the boundary policed violently.

### 1.3 Projective Identification

**Mechanism.** He places his own unconscious contents into others and then relates to those others as if they contained them. He projects *fear* (everyone in his presence is meant to feel what he refuses to) and *weakness* (every adversary is contemptible, soft, decadent — a description that maps onto whatever in himself he has foreclosed). The classical secondary move — pressuring the target to *enact* the projected content — is one of his signature interrogation tactics: he provokes the victim into the cowering, pleading, or rage-display he has assigned them, then treats the elicited behavior as confirmation.

**Behavioral signature.** Taunting that has the structure of *coaching* — he tells the victim what they are about to be, then makes them be it. The Diamondback captivity arc reads, in retrospect, as a sustained projective-identification exercise: he needed her terror to be evidence of his potency, and her partial refusal to deliver clean terror was the unmetabolizable insult that produced the obsession.

### 1.4 Denial *(specifically, denial of one's own affective states)*

**Mechanism.** Rumlow does not appear to register, or refuses to register, his own fear, grief, shame, and humiliation. This is not bravado; bravado implies the affect is felt and overridden. In Rumlow the disavowal is upstream of feeling — the affect is denied entry to consciousness in the first place, or is reflexively converted to anger before it is processed.

**Behavioral signature.** Post-disfigurement conduct is the cleanest specimen. A face burned to ruin would produce, in nearly any human nervous system, a documented depressive interval — withdrawal, mirror-avoidance, sleep disturbance, suicidal ideation. Rumlow shows none of this in the canon. He returns to operational tempo immediately. Either the affects are absent (unlikely — the structures are intact) or they are denied at the threshold. The mask is not denial's symbol; the mask is denial's *device* — it removes the daily mirror-confrontation that would force the affect into awareness.

### 1.5 Acting Out

**Mechanism.** Internal pressures are discharged into external behavior without intermediate symbolization. He does not dream-work, fantasize, or rehearse internally; he *does*. This is the most reliable single feature of his cognitive-emotional metabolism.

**Behavioral signature.** Affective escalation produces immediate motor expression. When the Skull is endangered or insulted, Rumlow moves — he does not seethe, plan, or write a letter. When sexual or possessive impulses arise, he acquires. When humiliated, he kills. The internal landscape is converted directly into the external environment with extremely short latency.

### 1.6 Omnipotent Control

**Mechanism.** Maintenance of the fantasy that the operational environment is, in principle, controllable through force and will. Failures of control are attributed to insufficient force rather than to limits of control as such.

**Behavioral signature.** No documented retreat from a target once committed; willingness to absorb tactical losses to maintain the appearance of inexorable progression. The repeated returns at Diamondback are the ledger entry on this defense — the project of possessing her cannot be abandoned, because abandoning it would admit a limit.

### 1.7 Devaluation

**Mechanism.** Targets and adversaries are pre-emptively reduced in worth so that whatever he does to them is congruent with their value. Civilians are not really alive in the relevant sense; liberals, the soft, the merciful, are sub-strength humans whose suffering carries no moral weight.

**Behavioral signature.** Verbal register in combat is heavily devaluative — the taunts are not just insults, they are *ontological demotions*. He doesn't tell Cap he will lose; he tells Cap what Cap *is*, in the contemptuous-anthropological mode. This is also why he is impervious to moral appeals: the appealer has been pre-demoted to a category whose moral speech does not register.

### 1.8 Primitive Idealization (single object, persistent)

**Mechanism.** Allocation of all admiration-capacity to a single object (the Skull-line), with consequent freedom from the ambivalence that distributed idealization would generate. He is *not* idealizing-and-devaluing in the BPD oscillation; he idealizes once, durably, and devalues everyone else as a constant background.

**Behavioral signature.** Decades of unbroken service through body-swaps, deaths, daughter-succession, and proxy-incarnations. The cleanness of the transfer from Skull to Sin to Hydra-Cap is diagnostic: the *position* is what's idealized, not the occupant, which is why the idealization is unkillable.

---

## 2. The Mid-Level — Defenses Present but Subordinate

### 2.1 Sadism as Affect Regulator

Strictly speaking sadism is a drive expression, not a defense; in Rumlow it has been *recruited into defensive function*. Inflicting suffering reliably down-regulates whatever internal pressure he carries. It is therefore his primary self-soothing mechanism — the functional analogue of what a less organized subject would do with alcohol, food, or sex. (His asceticism around substances is partly explained by this: he does not need them; he has a better regulator.)

**Behavioral signature.** Operational tempo *increases* under stress rather than degrading, because each act of inflicted violence discharges the stress. He is, paradoxically, at his most stable while doing his most extreme work.

### 2.2 Counterphobic Action

**Mechanism.** Whatever the system flags as threatening, he moves toward rather than away from. This is partly identification-with-aggressor (becoming the threat) and partly a discrete defense (depriving fear of its object by overrunning it).

**Behavioral signature.** Willing engagement with super-powered adversaries against whom his survival probability is poor; deliberate close-quarter work where range would be safer; the habit of removing the mask in private but never in public — the public exposure being the one threat-axis he cannot overrun by approach.

### 2.3 Somatic Discipline as Defense

**Mechanism.** Daily, ritualized control of the body — conditioning, weapons drill, weight discipline — functions defensively by producing a continuous proprioceptive evidence stream that he is *intact, powerful, present*. The body is the screen on which he reads his ongoing existence; if the body performs, the existence is secured.

**Behavioral signature.** Maintenance of peak unenhanced human conditioning into his forties, despite a face that no longer needs to be presentable and a life that no longer requires civilian fitness. The discipline is for him, not for any audience.

### 2.4 Role Consolidation (the Mask as Prosthetic Ego-Boundary)

**Mechanism.** Post-disfigurement, the skull mask absorbs the function of social skin — the surface through which a person is recognized, addressed, and held in others' minds. The mask is not concealment; it is *substitution*. It supplies a fixed, legible identity that does not require the labor of self-presentation.

**Behavioral signature.** Continuous wear. Retention of the persona during periods when tactical concealment would favor a civilian face. Resistance to the Pleasant Hill restoration when it is revealed — the false civilian identity is experienced as theft, not gift, because it removes the prosthesis.

### 2.5 Hierarchical Submission as Anxiety Containment

**Mechanism.** Being commanded is, for Rumlow, relieving. The presence of a worthy superior resolves the ambiguity that would otherwise have to be tolerated. He outsources existential authorship to the Skull-line and is thereby relieved of the burden of generating meaning.

**Behavioral signature.** Visible decrease in residual restlessness when in the Skull's or Sin's presence; tactical patience extends; ideological doubt — never abundant — drops to zero. Conversely, intervals without a clear superior (interregnum periods after the Skull's apparent deaths) produce a more chaotic, less effective Rumlow.

---

## 3. Defenses Notably Absent (Diagnostically Significant)

The absences are as informative as the presences. A subject of this combat exposure and trauma load *should* show:

- **Repression** — not visible. He does not appear to bury content; the content is either acted out, denied at threshold, or simply not generated.
- **Reaction formation** — absent. He does not convert hostility into ostentatious kindness, or desire into ostentatious chastity. He *is* what he feels.
- **Sublimation** — absent. There is no productive, socially-acceptable channel into which his aggressive drive is diverted. The drive goes where it goes.
- **Intellectualization** — absent. He does not theorize his violence, his ideology, or himself. (Contrast Zemo, who intellectualizes constantly.)
- **Humor** — present only in the sadistic register (taunting, gallows-cruelty). The mature defensive humor that integrates painful truth is not in his repertoire.
- **Altruism** — absent at the defensive level; the apparent self-sacrifices on behalf of the Skull-line are loyalty-acts, not altruism.
- **Anticipation** (the mature defense of preparing for foreseeable painful affect) — absent in the affective sense; present only operationally, which is not the same thing. He anticipates *threats*, not *feelings*.
- **Suppression** (conscious, temporary setting-aside of affect) — not visible because there is no observed affect to suppress.
- **Somatization** — absent. He does not convert distress into bodily symptom. The body is an instrument and a fortress; it is not allowed to speak distress.
- **Dissociation** — not observed in the clinical sense. He is fully present during violence; he does not fugue, depersonalize, or amnesia. His "split" is between persons, not within himself.

The clinical reading of these absences: Rumlow's psyche is not organized to *contain* affect. It is organized to *discharge* it. The defenses that exist to bind and hold internal pressure are simply not built into the structure, because the structure does not retain the pressure long enough to need them.

---

## 4. Compensatory Mechanisms — Positive (Ego-Syntonic Strengths)

These are adaptive in the sense that they *work* — they produce competence, durability, and operational value within his chosen ecology. Their moral valence is a separate question.

### 4.1 Discipline of Self in Service of Other

Most antisocial subjects fail at sustained discipline because the rewards of impulse outweigh the rewards of the long game. Rumlow does not — because the long game *is* the Skull, and the Skull-reward is greater than any impulse-reward. This produces a uniquely durable operator: physically conditioned, technically maintained, behaviorally consistent across decades. The compensation is real: he has more impulse control than most of his diagnostic peers.

### 4.2 Tactical Patience

The corollary capacity. He can wait — for the right shot (the Courthouse rifle), for the right opening, for the right humiliation of the right enemy. The patience is real but conditional; it is sustained by the certainty that the wait serves the cause. Patience without ideological scaffolding would not be available to him.

### 4.3 Technical Excellence

His career as senior instructor at Taskmaster's academy — early-twenties competence sufficient to teach professional killers — is not a footnote. Rumlow has *invested in skill* the way an artisan does. Firearms, demolitions, edged weapons, hand-to-hand, infiltration, interrogation. Each of these is a separate study, separately maintained. This is compensatory in the precise sense: it produces a competence-based self-worth that does not depend on the moment-to-moment validation most personalities like his require.

### 4.4 Ego-Subordination Capacity

Rare in his typology. He can be told *no*, by the Skull or by Sin, and accept it. He can take a supporting role without resentment when the cause requires it. This is the compensatory benefit of the idealization-of-other defense: by emptying himself of ambition for the top seat, he is freed from the destabilizing competitive jealousies that destroy similar operators.

### 4.5 Recovery from Setback

He does not, behaviorally, ruminate. Defeats are filed and the next operation is undertaken. The capacity is partly a function of denial (no affect to ruminate on) and partly a function of role consolidation (the role is intact even when the engagement was lost). The result is a low-drag operator who can be tasked repeatedly without the morale degradation usually seen in repeated failure.

---

## 5. Compensatory Mechanisms — Negative (Adaptations That Foreclose)

These are the costs paid for the above strengths — adaptations that solve a problem at the price of closing a developmental door.

### 5.1 Sadism as Sole Reward Channel

What started as a drive expression has, over decades, *outcompeted* every other potential source of pleasure. He no longer has access to the small-bandwidth rewards — companionship without dominance, food without ceremony, sex without coercion, work without violence. The reward system has narrowed to a single channel of high amplitude. The compensation is total stability; the cost is total foreclosure of the human reward landscape.

### 5.2 Possession-Schema for Women

The Diamondback structure — woman as object-to-be-acquired, her terror as confirmation of acquisition — is not a phase he passed through. It is the entire architecture of his heterosexual relating, and it has prevented any non-coercive partnership from forming. The partnership with Sin is the closest approach to mutuality, and even it is mediated by shared dominance over others, not by the experience of being equals.

### 5.3 Identity-Prosthesis Dependency (The Mask)

The mask works — it stabilizes a post-disfigurement self that would otherwise have to be rebuilt. The cost is that the prosthesis becomes load-bearing: removal is now a destabilization. He cannot return to a civilian face even if a civilian face becomes available, because the architecture has grown around the prosthesis.

### 5.4 Single-Object Idealization

The idealization of the Skull-line gives him everything — meaning, regulation, identity, mission. The cost is the brittleness that always accompanies single-point dependency. If the Skull-line is decisively shown to have used and discarded him, there is no second narrative. He has invested all of meaning in one position and built no diversified holdings.

### 5.5 Foreclosure of Lateral Bonding

He has no friends. The capacity is not damaged — it is *unbuilt*. He never developed the lateral-bond machinery; the Crims taught vertical relating; the Skull confirmed it. The compensatory benefit is freedom from peer-conflict and divided loyalty; the cost is the absence of any relational redundancy when the vertical lines break.

### 5.6 Outward-Facing Defense System

The entire defensive architecture is built to manage the external world's perception of him and to discharge internal pressure outward. He is undefended *inward* — has no machinery for self-examination, self-comfort, or self-repair. As long as he is operational, this is invisible. In a confinement scenario (prison, captivity, immobilization) where he cannot discharge outward, the system has nowhere to route the pressure, and there is no internal apparatus to absorb it. This is the structural condition under which a Rumlow decompensation is most likely.

### 5.7 Operational-Only Cognition

His intelligence has been heavily specialized into the operational domain — tactics, logistics, tradecraft, terrain-reading. The cost is the atrophy or non-development of every other mode: no aesthetic, no abstract, no historical, no introspective. He cannot think his way out of a non-operational problem because he has no non-operational thinking. The compensation is excellence in his domain; the foreclosure is everything outside it.

---

## 6. Ranked Synthesis (Primitiveness → Maturity)

1. **Identification with the Aggressor** — load-bearing, character-fused.
2. **Splitting** — categorical, decades-stable.
3. **Denial (of own affect)** — at-threshold, pre-conscious.
4. **Projective Identification** — operationally weaponized.
5. **Acting Out** — short-latency motor discharge.
6. **Omnipotent Control** — limits attributed to insufficient force.
7. **Devaluation** — pre-emptive ontological demotion of others.
8. **Primitive Idealization (single object)** — durable, transferable, brittle.
9. **Sadism as Affect Regulator** — drive recruited to defense.
10. **Counterphobic Action** — approach toward what threatens.
11. **Somatic Discipline** — body as continuous proof of intactness.
12. **Role Consolidation (mask as prosthetic skin)** — identity offloaded to artifact.
13. **Hierarchical Submission** — anxiety outsourced to superior.

The list contains no defense at the neurotic or mature levels. The structure is **all floor, with engineered superstructure** — the persona, the discipline, the mask, the role — built directly on the primitive base, skipping the middle stories that most adults inhabit.

---

## 7. Operational Implications

- **Confinement degrades him.** Remove the outward discharge and the inward absence of containment becomes visible. Long-term solitary confinement, in particular, would not break him into remorse — it would degrade him into a less organized, less effective version of himself.
- **The mask is non-negotiable.** Any attempt to engage him without it (forced unmasking, civilian-face restoration) is read as assault on the self, not as access to the self.
- **Moral appeal is structurally inaudible.** The appealer is pre-demoted; the speech does not register as moral speech.
- **Substitution wounds.** Replacement in the enforcer role by a preferred figure produces a wound that physical injury does not.
- **The single decisive lever** is the integrity of the idealized object. Corrupting the Skull-line's relationship to him — not killing the Skull, which only consolidates martyrdom, but *demonstrating that the Skull-line used him as a disposable instrument* — is the one move against which his architecture has no defense, because the architecture is built on the assumption that the idealization is reciprocated by being *worthy of his service*. The defense system can survive his being hurt; it cannot survive his being *cheap*.

— END SECTION.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — BROCK RUMLOW

## Methodological Preface

This section reconstructs Rumlow's clinical psychological picture across five developmental epochs, tracking three core dimensions — **affect regulation, cognitive style, self-concept** — and a set of subsidiary dimensions (defensive organization, mentalization, relational schemata, identity coherence, moral cognition) decade by decade. The frameworks invoked are the standard ones: Kernberg's structural model of personality organization (identity diffusion, defensive level, reality testing); Cleckley/Hare's two-factor psychopathy construct; Fonagy/Bateman's mentalization model; Bowlby/Main attachment classifications; Linehan's emotion-regulation taxonomy; and the McWilliams/PDM-2 schema for character diagnosis. None of these instruments was ever administered to the subject; the inferences below are derived from observable conduct cited to the published record.

The headline finding the longitudinal data supports: Rumlow is one of the most **structurally stable** antisocial personalities in the catalog. He does not develop in the ordinary sense. He **consolidates**. The arc is not change; it is hardening, with one significant inflection (the disfigurement) that does not redirect the trajectory but accelerates and externalizes it.

---

## EPOCH I — Adolescence to Early Twenties: Lower East Side, Savage Crims, Flight (c. age 14–22)

**Affect regulation.** The earliest available behavioral data — the gang-leadership period culminating in the sexual assault, the murder of a rival's family, and the killing of the avenging father and crippling of the sister — establishes a juvenile affective profile that is already aberrant by reference to any developmental norm. Most adolescents engaged in extreme group violence display either pre-act dysregulation (rage build-up, perceived provocation, intoxication-mediated disinhibition) or post-act dysregulation (panic, dissociation, somatic distress, sleep disturbance, the characteristic juvenile-offender "freeze" in custody). Rumlow exhibits **neither pole**. The acts are perpetrator-initiated rather than reactive; the post-act behavior is logistical (flight) rather than affective (collapse). This is the signature of what the juvenile-forensic literature labels **callous-unemotional traits** — a developmental precursor band predictive, in longitudinal samples, of adult psychopathy in the Factor-1-heavy register. In Linehan's vocabulary, his baseline emotional intensity appears *low to moderate* with a *slow return to baseline only because the deflection from baseline was minimal to begin with.* This is not a child who is "hot." This is a child who is *cold and active*.

**Cognitive style.** Already concrete-operational, instrumentally rational, and morally unencumbered. The decision to flee the country at ~17 evidences a forward-planning capacity unusual for the developmental window and the milieu. He does not blunder into capture; he calculates exit. There is no documentation of academic engagement, intellectual interests, or symbolic life of any kind. Cognition is wholly **dorsal-stream tactical**: terrain, targets, exits, weapons. The world is parsed as a field of dominance gradients.

**Self-concept.** Forming, but already oriented along the axis it will occupy for the rest of his life: *I am the strongest thing in this room.* The Crims provide the first social mirror that confirms it. Critically, there is no evidence of a competing pre-criminal self — no civilian aspiration, no faith identity, no school identity, no romantic identity — that the gang identity displaces. The gang identity is the *first* identity, and the adult Crossbones identity will be its smooth continuation.

**Defensive organization.** Already **primitive-borderline level** by Kernberg's criteria: splitting, projective identification, omnipotence, devaluation. But — and this is unusual — without the identity diffusion that ordinarily accompanies this defensive level. The personality is borderline-level in its *defenses* and integrated in its *identity*. This is the structural signature of the **malignant-narcissistic / antisocial** organization, distinct from the borderline organization proper.

**Mentalization.** Cognitive theory of mind intact and instrumentalized — he reads the rival's father's predictable revenge response and prepares the ambush. Affective mentalization — the capacity to *feel into* another's state — selectively offline. The sister's terror is not registered as an aversive social signal; it does not deter, in fact it may be already proto-reinforcing.

**Attachment.** Best classified as **disorganized in infancy reorganized into coercive-controlling in adolescence** — the pattern Main and others have documented in children of severely neglectful or absent caregivers who later seize control of their social environment through aggression. There are no canonically named parents, siblings, or protective adults. The absence itself is the datum.

---

## EPOCH II — Exile and Professionalization: Taskmaster's Academy through Early Skull Service (c. age 22–30)

**Affect regulation.** The defining acquisition of this period is **professionalization of arousal**. Whatever raw violence Rumlow brought to the Crims was undisciplined relative to the standard required to instruct at a mercenary academy. The fact that he becomes the senior instructor — not a student who graduates, but the teacher of professional killers — implies a remarkable downward titration of affective noise during violent action. He learns, or it is revealed he already possesses, the operator's holy grail: **tonic calm under acute threat**, the parasympathetic-dominant violence that distinguishes a professional from a brawler. Heart rate variability under fire is, of course, not measured; the behavioral proxy is the *quality* of his technique under load, which canon consistently rates at near-elite.

**Cognitive style.** Expands from street-tactical to **operational-strategic**. He learns infiltration, demolitions, edged-weapon work, marksmanship, small-unit command, counterintelligence. He acquires the syntax of professional violence. Notably, the expansion is *bounded*: he does not develop interests in finance, politics-as-discipline, languages-beyond-instrumental, art, history-beyond-Skull-mythology. The cognitive growth is fully sublimated to the operator role. This is one of his stable signatures across the whole life: **deep within domain, blank without**.

**Self-concept.** The first major consolidation. He moves from "strongest in the room" to "professional among professionals, and best among them." This is also the period in which he is *selected by the Red Skull* — a moment whose psychological weight cannot be overstated. For a young man with no prior introjected paternal figure, recognition by an authoritarian patriarch of mythic stature provides the **organizing introject** the structure has been waiting for. Object-relations theory would describe this as the late-installation of a father-imago into a developmental cavity. The introject is not nurturing; it is *commissioning*. Rumlow is now an *instrument*, and being an instrument of the right hand is, for him, the highest possible self-concept.

**Defensive organization.** **Identification with the aggressor** stabilizes as the master defense. The Skull is the most feared man in the world Rumlow can perceive; becoming the Skull's hand is the most complete identification with the aggressor available to him. The defense is so effective at organizing his anxiety that it forecloses the development of higher-order defenses. He will never need to repress, sublimate, or intellectualize, because he never experiences the kind of unbearable affect those defenses are evolved to manage.

**Mentalization.** Cognitive mentalization sharpens dramatically under Taskmaster's tutelage — reading combatants, predicting movement, anticipating responses. Affective mentalization remains weaponized rather than relational: he uses what he understands of fear to *produce* fear, not to *avoid* producing it.

---

## EPOCH III — Mature Operator: Field Command, Diamondback, Body-Swap Conspiracies (c. age 30–40, Gruenwald-era canon)

**Affect regulation.** Operational regulation is now elite and stable. The novel finding in this epoch is the **Diamondback signal**: a single relational object whose presence and absence demonstrably modulate his behavior outside the baseline. The captivity arc reveals an affective register otherwise undocumented — a kind of *fixated, perseverative possessiveness* that does not fit the cold-operator profile cleanly. The most parsimonious reading: Rumlow's reward system, organized almost entirely around dominance-cruelty, has a small and highly specific subsystem keyed to *sustained possession* of a sexual object. Diamondback activates it. Her later defection to Cap is not, for him, a romantic injury (he is incapable of romantic injury in the affective sense); it is a **property tort**. The affective coloration is closer to a collector's rage at a stolen specimen than to a jilted lover's grief. But the perseveration is real, and it persists across decades — meaning the system, however cold, has *memory*.

**Cognitive style.** Now a planner of multi-stage operations involving political assassination, body-swap conspiracies, and clandestine logistics across the Hydra/Kubekult/Skull-network. The cognitive style remains concrete and operational, but the *scale* expands. He does not engage with the ideological content of the Skull's projects — there is no evidence he ever debates Aryan-supremacist or Nietzschean doctrine; he simply transmits and executes. This is the **executive without the executive function for self-direction** — supremely competent at the *how*, structurally uninterested in the *why*.

**Self-concept.** Stable, consolidated, grandiose. He now experiences himself as a peer of the elite operators (Bullseye, Taskmaster, the assassin demimonde) and the *favored* enforcer of the world's most feared man. There is no evidence of the inflation-deflation cycling that characterizes fragile narcissism. The grandiosity does not require constant feeding because it is structurally anchored to the Skull's recognition, which is reliably provided.

**Moral cognition.** At Kohlberg's pre-conventional level functionally, but organized into a *pseudo-conventional* shell by Skull-ideology — i.e., he does not reason from internalized principles, he reasons from *Skull's-will-as-law*. This functional substitution of an external authoritarian schedule for an internal moral compass is the signature of the **authoritarian character** in the Adorno/Fromm tradition. Rumlow is its forensic exemplar.

**Defenses.** Splitting now operates at the **macropolitical** level — the world is divided into Skull-aligned and Skull-opposed, with Cap as the canonical opposed-figure. **Devaluation** is the constant register applied to non-aligned humans, particularly civilians (whose suffering is below notice) and liberal-aligned heroes (whose restraint is read as weakness).

---

## EPOCH IV — The Assassination of Rogers, Disfigurement, and Mask-Integration (c. age 40–45, Brubaker-era canon)

This is the **inflection epoch** — the only period in the longitudinal record where significant structural events occur. There are two: the killing of Steve Rogers, and the burn injury.

**Affect regulation, pre-assassination.** Tonic calm under the most operationally consequential mission of his life. The execution is technically precise; he pulls the trigger himself rather than delegating, which is psychologically diagnostic — he wants the act to be *his*, not because of public credit (he is masked) but because possession of the kill is the deepest dialect of his self-concept. The kill itself produces no documented destabilization; he is captured, interrogated, extracted, resumes operations.

**Affect regulation, post-disfigurement.** The most clinically interesting non-event in the record. Severe facial burns with permanent disfigurement produce, in nearly any clinical population, a predictable cluster: acute stress symptoms, body-image disturbance, social withdrawal, depressive episode, often suicidal ideation, often substance use as anesthesia. Rumlow shows **none of this**. The absence is not subtle; across the post-Reborn run, his operational tempo increases, his identification with the Crossbones role tightens, and the mask becomes *welcomed* rather than *imposed*. The clinical reading: a self that was already organized around being-a-symbol-of-fear *experiences the disfigurement as confirmatory rather than threatening*. The injury matches the persona. The mask is no longer concealing a face he prefers; it is presenting a face he prefers. In PDM-2 terms, this is a personality with an **ego-syntonic relationship to its own monstrosity**, and trauma to the body that confirms the monstrosity is therefore not traumatic in the clinical sense at all. This is also why he meets none of the PTSD criteria despite a trauma exposure history that, by ordinary actuarial standards, would yield diagnosable PTSD with very high probability.

**Cognitive style.** Unchanged in kind, intensified in pace. The post-Reborn period shows him executing operations with a slightly *less* patient signature than before — the disfigurement appears to have shortened his fuse, though only at the margin. This is consistent with cumulative TBI burden plus chronic neuropathic pain plus the psychological consolidation that *makes patience less necessary to him* because his identity is now externally guaranteed by the mask.

**Self-concept.** This is the period of **completion**. The Brock-Rumlow-residual that occupied some small psychic real estate beneath the Crossbones identity is functionally extinguished. The mask becomes face, the persona becomes person. There is no longer a civilian self to return to — and no evidence the subject experiences this as a loss. Identity coherence reaches its maximum.

**Relational pattern.** The **Sin partnership** matures into the closest thing to a peer bond in his entire life. The structural geometry is critical: Sin is the Skull's daughter, the Skull-line incarnate in female form, both sexual partner and ideological co-religionist. For Rumlow she resolves the otherwise irreconcilable: a sexual relationship that does not require him to relate horizontally (because she is, by Skull-succession, vertically positioned above him in the cause hierarchy). The bond is mutual within their idiom, but the idiom is *shared violence*. Sex and killing are paired stimuli; there is no documented domestic, restful, or playful register to the relationship.

**Defenses.** Identification with the aggressor reaches its apotheosis when the aggressor (the Skull) is, intermittently, *dead or displaced* — and Rumlow does not destabilize. He transfers the identification to Sin/Skadi without seam. This reveals that the introject was never the *person* of Schmidt; it was the *line*. Object-relations stability of a high order around an antisocial-malignant core.

---

## EPOCH V — Post-Disfigurement Late Career: Fear Itself, Uncanny Avengers, Pleasant Hill, Secret Empire (c. age 45–50+, Remender / Spencer canon)

**Affect regulation.** Stable at the elite-operator baseline, with the slightly-shortened fuse persisting. The interesting late-career datum is **Pleasant Hill**: imprisoned by the Cosmic Cube fragment Kobik, given a wholly synthesized civilian identity, restored to apparent normalcy. When the synthesized identity dissolves and the Crossbones identity reasserts, there is no evidence of grief for the civilian life he briefly led — no perseverative reference to the woman he was with in the false town, no nostalgia, no ambivalence about returning to operations. The clinical interpretation: the synthesized civilian self was experienced, retrospectively, as a costume; the Crossbones self is felt as **ontologically prior and real**. This is the same psychological structure as his relationship to the mask — what most subjects experience as core, he experiences as imposition; what most subjects experience as mask, he experiences as core.

**Cognitive style.** Now operating in a more chaotic narrative environment (the Hydra-Cap succession), Rumlow demonstrates the cognitive economy of his concrete-operational fascism: he does not require the leader to *be* the Skull, only to be the *Skull's project*. He absorbs the Hydra-Cap proposition without ideological friction because his cognitive style was never engaged with content in the first place; it was engaged with *line*. The cognitive style has not developed; it has been *vindicated by circumstance* as efficient for his needs.

**Self-concept.** Continued consolidation. Now functioning as elder-statesman muscle within the Hydra-aligned periphery — a senior figure to younger operators, a known quantity to the Skull-line leadership. The grandiosity is the most stable variable in the entire profile across all epochs.

**Mentalization.** Cognitive mentalization remains operational and weaponized; affective mentalization remains absent. He has not learned, across decades of intimate relating with Sin, to feel-into another's distress as aversive. He has only refined his capacity to *produce* distress with surgical specificity.

**Moral cognition.** Unmoved across the lifespan from authoritarian-substitution morality. He has had every opportunity that life offers a senior operator to develop a private skepticism — disillusionment with command, recognition of betrayal, observed cruelty toward favored subordinates — and there is no evidence he has ever entertained it. His moral structure is not *closed against doubt* (which would imply doubt being repressed); it is **constitutionally without the receptor for doubt** at the values level.

**Defenses.** Late-career stability of the same primitive defenses: splitting, projective identification, devaluation, identification with the aggressor. No higher-order defensive layer has emerged. This is itself diagnostic — psychological development across the adult lifespan in healthy and even in many disordered subjects involves the gradual layering of mature defenses (humor, sublimation, anticipation, altruism) atop the primitive ones. Rumlow has acquired *none*. He is, in this respect, the same psychological organism at fifty that he was at twenty-two.

---

## CROSS-EPOCH SYNTHESIS

**Affect regulation, longitudinal arc.** Baseline tonic calm under operational load, present from earliest available data, professionalized through his twenties to elite standard, marginally degraded by cumulative neurological insult and the post-disfigurement consolidation. The single reliable disregulator across all epochs is **threat to or insult against the Skull-line**, including by extension the Sin-partnership, with a secondary disregulator being **the denied/escaped possession** (Diamondback as the only individuated instance). The regulation is **borrowed from the cause** — it is the steadiness of a man whose anxieties have been outsourced to an external organizing object. This is the dimension on which he is most exploitable: corrupt the object, and the regulation has no internal substrate to fall back on.

**Cognitive style, longitudinal arc.** Concrete-operational throughout, expanding in scale (street → professional → strategic → command-peripheral) but never in *kind*. No emergent symbolic, abstract, or reflective dimension across the lifespan. Cognitive mentalization elite within domain, weaponized; affective mentalization persistently offline. **Ideologically credulous within authoritarian frame**, ideologically incurious without it. The cognitive profile is that of an executive operator whose intelligence has been wholly devoted to the *how* of mission and never to the *whether*.

**Self-concept, longitudinal arc.** Stable, grandiose, martial, *consolidating monotonically* across the lifespan. Three reinforcement events: selection by the Skull (Epoch II), execution of Rogers (Epoch IV), disfigurement-into-mask (Epoch IV). One null event where development would be expected: the Pleasant Hill civilian-identity exposure produces no retained ambivalence (Epoch V). The self-concept is the most structurally rigid variable in the profile.

**The single longitudinal finding that organizes the file.** Rumlow does not develop; he *crystallizes*. The frameworks clinicians use to track adult psychological development — defensive maturation, identity integration through midlife reappraisal, generativity, affective deepening, moral broadening, the late-life relaxation of grandiosity — produce, when applied to him, *flat lines*. The closest analogy in the clinical literature is the long-followed cohort of incarcerated psychopaths in the Hare studies, in whom standard developmental indices show minimal change across decades while operational sophistication continues to refine. Rumlow is that organism with an authoritarian movement attached, which is the configuration in which the type does its most historically consequential damage.

The corollary, and the closing analytic note for this section: every intervention model premised on the discovery of a buried developmental wound — a childhood self that can be reached, a moment of redirection that can be exploited, a grief that can be activated — runs aground on the same fact. There is no buried self. The self that the surveillance file traces is the only self that was ever there, refining its expression, finding its scaffolding, and at last fully fused with the mask it always preferred.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT: BROCK RUMLOW

*UATU Dossier, Section 4 of the Behavioral Volume. Cross-reference §§1 (History), 2 (Medical), 3 (Psychological), 5 (Personality Synthesis). All diagnostic frames given in DSM-5-TR/ICD-11 analogs; legacy descriptors retained where clinically useful. This is a longitudinal, evidence-anchored psychiatric workup, not a charge sheet.*

---

## 4.1 FRAMING THE ASSESSMENT

A psychiatric workup of Brock Rumlow is unusual in one specific respect: most subjects of comparable seriousness — career operators, terror cadres, ideological killers — show diagnostic *layering*. There is the personality substrate, and there are episodic disorders sitting on top of it: a depressive episode after a loss, a substance use disorder secondary to occupational stress, a trauma-related disorder after a particular incident. The clinical picture is a stack.

Rumlow does not present this way. The record, traced from the Gruenwald origin material (Captain America #359-362) forward through more than three decades of published incident, shows a remarkably *thin* psychiatric profile in the Axis-I/episodic-disorder sense, and a remarkably *thick* one in the personality-disorder sense. He is, to use the older language, almost pure character pathology. The interesting psychiatric questions about him are not "what episode is he in" but "what is the precise architecture of the personality, and what differential diagnoses do we have to clear to be sure we have named it correctly."

That is the work of this section.

---

## 4.2 PRINCIPAL DIAGNOSTIC IMPRESSION

**Antisocial Personality Disorder (DSM-5-TR 301.7 / ICD-11 6D10.2 with dissocial features), severe, with prominent psychopathic features (Hare PCL-R Factor 1 dominant), and a sadistic specifier in the legacy DSM-III-R sense.**

This is the primary diagnosis. It is held with high confidence. The evidentiary base is one of the densest in the rogues' catalog.

### 4.2.1 Criterion-by-criterion walkthrough (DSM-5-TR ASPD)

The diagnosis requires (a) a pervasive pattern of disregard for and violation of the rights of others since age 15, with at least three of seven specified features; (b) age ≥18; (c) evidence of Conduct Disorder with onset before age 15; (d) the conduct is not exclusively during the course of Schizophrenia or Bipolar Disorder.

- **Failure to conform to social norms with respect to lawful behaviors:** the entire occupational record is a list of indictable acts spanning homicide, terrorism, kidnapping, torture, conspiracy, illegal weapons possession, and treason analogs. Fully satisfied.
- **Deceitfulness — repeated lying, use of aliases, conning others for personal profit or pleasure:** documented aliases (Crossbones, Bender, the Frank Simpson disambiguation noise in early files); tradecraft involves deception by definition; manipulation of Diamondback under the guise of romantic interest in the Gruenwald arc. Satisfied.
- **Impulsivity or failure to plan ahead:** this criterion sits uneasily. Rumlow is not *impulsive*; he is one of the more disciplined planners in the field. However, the criterion is met in the *micro-impulsive* register — sexual aggression in the Crims era, opportunistic violence when the structure permits it. Partially satisfied via the early record; mature presentation downweights this item, which is part of why the case is more Factor-1 than Factor-2.
- **Irritability and aggressiveness, as indicated by repeated physical fights or assaults:** trivially satisfied.
- **Reckless disregard for safety of self or others:** the safety-of-others prong is overwhelmed by evidence. The safety-of-self prong is more interesting — Rumlow takes calculated risks but is not a thrill-seeker in the sensation-seeking sense; he goes into objectively dangerous engagements with adequate preparation. He has been wounded repeatedly because his work is dangerous, not because he is reckless. Satisfied via the others-prong.
- **Consistent irresponsibility, as indicated by repeated failure to sustain consistent work behavior or honor financial obligations:** *failed.* This is the criterion that distinguishes Rumlow from the prototypical ASPD presentation. He has sustained one employment relationship — service to the Skull-line — for the entirety of his adult life. He is, in the mercenary world, a *reliable employee*. This is diagnostically informative and we return to it below.
- **Lack of remorse, as indicated by being indifferent to or rationalizing having hurt, mistreated, or stolen from another:** the most floridly satisfied criterion in the record. There is no documented instance of post-conduct remorse across thirty-plus years.

Five of seven met, comfortably exceeding the threshold of three. Conduct Disorder before 15 satisfied by the Savage Crims material — group sexual assault, multiple homicides, and the maiming of the rival's sister, all in his mid-teens. Age threshold satisfied. No primary psychotic or mood disorder accounting for the conduct. **Diagnosis: confirmed.**

### 4.2.2 Severity specifier

Severity in ASPD is conventionally indexed by the count and intensity of violations, the breadth of contexts in which the pattern manifests, and the degree of functional impairment to others. By all three indices Rumlow is in the **severe** range. The PCL-R analog, were one to be scored on the record, would place him in the high-30s/low-40s — well above the conventional threshold of 30 for psychopathy in North American forensic samples.

### 4.2.3 The Factor-1/Factor-2 architecture

Hare's two-factor model separates the interpersonal/affective features (Factor 1: glibness, grandiosity, pathological lying, lack of remorse, shallow affect, callousness, failure to accept responsibility) from the antisocial-lifestyle features (Factor 2: need for stimulation, parasitic lifestyle, poor behavioral controls, early behavior problems, lack of realistic goals, impulsivity, irresponsibility, juvenile delinquency, revocation of conditional release, criminal versatility).

Rumlow's profile is **Factor-1 dominant**. He is high on every Factor-1 facet. He is high on the developmental items of Factor 2 (early behavior problems, juvenile delinquency, criminal versatility) but low on the *adult-lifestyle* items (parasitic lifestyle, impulsivity, poor behavioral controls, lack of realistic goals). His antisociality is *organized*, *career-shaped*, *goal-coherent*. This matches what the forensic literature calls the **"successful psychopath"** typology, with one important qualifier: in Rumlow's case "success" is purchased not by white-collar concealment but by *institutional encapsulation* inside an authoritarian organization that pays him to do exactly what his temperament wants done. He does not have to mask in civilian life because his employer rewards the unmasked self. This is the rarer and more dangerous Factor-1-dominant presentation.

### 4.2.4 Sadistic features

The DSM-III-R included Sadistic Personality Disorder in its appendix; it was removed from DSM-IV onward, but remains in clinical use as a descriptor and is partially captured by the cruelty facets of the ICD-11 dissocial pattern and the malevolent-aggression items of newer dimensional models (PID-5 callousness and hostility facets).

The criterion of intrinsic reinforcement is the test: is cruelty *instrumental* (used because it works) or *appetitive* (sought because it is pleasurable)? Rumlow meets the appetitive standard. The Diamondback captivity sequence is the cleanest specimen — the torture was operationally unnecessary at the durations and intensities he chose; the surplus is appetite. The taunting language with downed enemies, the theatricalization of kills, the documented preference for victims who can register what is being done to them, all point the same direction. **Sadistic specifier: confirmed.**

---

## 4.3 ETIOLOGY — A RECONSTRUCTIVE PSYCHIATRIC FORMULATION

The four-P case formulation (Predisposing, Precipitating, Perpetuating, Protective) provides a useful frame.

**Predisposing.** The record gives us no parents, no siblings, no protective adult, no developmental medical history. This negative space is itself data: an absence of any narrated protective figure across a published life of decades implies an actually absent or actively harmful early caregiving environment. We infer, with appropriate uncertainty, a developmentally neglectful or abusive context — Lower East Side, gang-saturated, no stabilizing institutional contact. Temperamentally, the early-onset cruelty and the absence of fearful reactivity to consequences suggest *low autonomic arousal at baseline* (the well-replicated finding in psychopathy research) and likely high callous-unemotional traits in childhood. Genetic loading cannot be assessed in the absence of family history, but the developmental phenotype is recognizable: a child with low fear, low empathic resonance, high reward-seeking, and no caregiver capable of channeling these into prosocial structure.

**Precipitating.** The Savage Crims is the first crystallizing context. A predatory peer hierarchy in adolescence is the worst possible "school" for a callous-unemotional child — it rewards exactly the traits that prosocial environments suppress, and provides the scaffolding (peer recognition, rank, sexual access via dominance) that converts diffuse cruelty into organized predation. The triggering incidents — the assault, the murders, the revenge killings, the flight from the country — close off any return path. By 17, the trajectory is fixed.

**Perpetuating.** Two factors. First, the **Taskmaster academy** — formal technical training transforms an effective predator into a professional one and embeds him in a labor market that pays for his pathology. Second, and far more important, the **capture by the Red Skull**. This is the etiologically critical event of the adult life. The Skull provides what Rumlow has never had: a vertical attachment object worthy (in his estimation) of submission, a coherent worldview that explains his existence to himself, a hierarchy that ranks him near the top, and an ongoing supply of sanctioned targets. The Skull's ideology is the *organizing introject* — not in the sense that Rumlow believes the doctrine intellectually (he does not engage with it intellectually at all) but in the sense that the doctrine provides the *holding structure* for his temperament. The personality crystallizes around the bond.

**Protective.** Functionally none. The disciplined work ethic and capacity for delayed gratification, which in a different developmental context would be protective traits, are here recruited entirely into the service of the pathological structure. There is no domain of his life — no hobby, no friendship, no civic attachment, no faith outside the Skull-frame — that operates as a counterweight.

The resulting formulation: **a constitutionally callous-unemotional child, developmentally unprotected and adolescently captured by a predatory peer ecology, who was then provided in young adulthood with an authoritarian institutional home that organized his temperament into its most stable and effective expression.** Nurture did not *create* the pathology; nurture *finished* it.

---

## 4.4 SYMPTOM PRESENTATION IN BEHAVIOR — THE OPERATIONAL READOUT

A clinical-list of features means little without behavioral specification. The following are the diagnostically relevant features as they appear in observable conduct.

- **Shallow affect:** facial expression (where the unmasked face is observable in flashback panels) is dominated by amusement, contempt, and aggressive arousal. The full register of sadness, tenderness, awe, gratitude, shame is absent from the record. With Sin, affect warms by one or two clicks — the closest he comes to tenderness — but never reaches the spectrum a clinician would call attached love. The mask, when adopted, makes this finding harder to assess by face; it does not change the underlying picture, which is also legible in voice register, body posture, and choice of words.
- **Glibness in operational contexts:** he can speak fluently and even charmingly when the task requires (early Diamondback approach work, certain undercover sequences). The glibness is thin — it does not survive sustained scrutiny by a perceptive interlocutor — but it is sufficient for short-duration tradecraft.
- **Pathological lying as professional skill:** lies are deployed without autonomic disturbance (no observable stress response, no tells), and are abandoned the moment they cease to be useful. He does not lie when truth serves him better; this is a *disciplined* psychopathy.
- **Grandiosity:** consolidated rather than fragile. He genuinely believes himself to be one of the most dangerous men alive, and the record largely supports the belief; the grandiosity is *calibrated to capability*, which is part of why it does not destabilize.
- **Lack of remorse:** total. No documented instance — not after the Crims-era atrocities, not after the Rogers assassination, not after the Xavier funeral attack, not after any of the casualty-heavy operations.
- **Failure to accept responsibility:** more nuanced than the prototypical presentation. He does not deny *authorship* of his acts (he is in fact proud of them); he denies *culpability* in the moral sense by refusing the framework that would generate culpability. Asked "did you do this," he says yes. Asked "was it wrong," the question fails to parse.
- **Callousness/lack of empathy:** affective empathy absent; cognitive empathy intact and weaponized. He reads people accurately enough to know precisely what frightens them, which is the operational signature of intact cognitive perspective-taking in the absence of affective resonance.
- **Need for stimulation:** present but channeled — not the bored, drifting sensation-seeking of the chaotic psychopath. He needs the stimulation his work provides and is content within it.
- **Stable identity:** rare in this population and clinically important. He knows who he is, has known for thirty years, and the disfigurement did not perturb the knowledge.

---

## 4.5 COMORBIDITY — WHAT ELSE IS THERE

The thinness of the psychiatric overlay is itself the central comorbidity finding. Items considered:

- **Mood disorders.** No evidence of Major Depressive Disorder at any point in the record, including the periods that would most predictably elicit it (capture, disfigurement, loss of the Skull, imprisonment in Pleasant Hill). No evidence of Persistent Depressive Disorder (he is not chronically dysthymic; baseline mood is amused-malevolent, not low). No evidence of Bipolar spectrum — no documented hypomanic or manic episodes, no decompensated mixed states; what reads as "high energy" is in fact his stable operating temperament. **Rule out: mood disorders, current and lifetime.**

- **Anxiety disorders.** No evidence of Generalized Anxiety, Panic, Social Anxiety, or specific phobia. Combat alertness is reality-based and dissipates appropriately when the threat passes. **Rule out.**

- **Trauma-and-stressor-related disorders.** Considered carefully because of the disfigurement and the cumulative violence exposure. Discussed in detail in §4.6 below; **ruled out** with explanation.

- **Substance use disorders.** No canonical pattern of alcohol or drug abuse. Of diagnostic note: psychopathic individuals often present with significant substance comorbidity (the disinhibited subtype especially); Rumlow's absence of substance pathology fits the disciplined Factor-1 profile and is consistent with the "successful" typology. He does not need to anesthetize. **Rule out, current and lifetime.**

- **Sexual disorders.** Coercive sexual behavior is documented and contributes to the ASPD/sadistic picture. Whether to additionally code a paraphilic disorder (Sexual Sadism Disorder, DSM-5-TR 302.84) is a close call. The criterion requires recurrent, intense sexual arousal from the physical or psychological suffering of another person, manifested by fantasies, urges, or behaviors, with either acted-on non-consenting partners or clinically significant distress/impairment. Acted-on non-consenting partners: present (Crims-era assault, Diamondback captivity). Recurrence and intensity: probable but not extensively documented in the published record. The cleanest reading is to code **Sexual Sadism Disorder, by history, provisional**, and treat the sadism more comprehensively under the ASPD-with-sadistic-features specifier rather than as a separate axis.

- **Neurocognitive sequelae.** Given the cumulative TBI burden plausible from his work history and the burn injury, *mild neurocognitive disorder* is on the differential as a future-development risk, but there is no current behavioral evidence — operational planning, language, memory for tradecraft details all appear preserved. **Subclinical at present; watch.**

- **Chronic pain.** Almost certainly present post-burn injury and post-cumulative-trauma; uncoded by the record because he does not report it, and personality-congruently denied. Of psychiatric relevance only in that untreated chronic pain often potentiates irritability and aggression — both of which he already has in abundance, making the contribution clinically invisible.

- **Personality comorbidity within Cluster B.** Sub-threshold narcissistic features are dense and contribute to the malignant-narcissistic flavor of the presentation, but a separate NPD diagnosis is not supported — see differential below. Sub-threshold paranoid features are *situational* (operational vigilance) rather than characterological.

---

## 4.6 RIGOROUS DIFFERENTIAL — WHAT HE IS NOT, AND WHY

This is the most important diagnostic work in the file, because the temptation to over-diagnose this subject is significant: he is florid, frightening, and has been through events that would, in most subjects, generate multiple Axis-I conditions. Discipline is required.

### 4.6.1 Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder (primary)

NPD requires a pervasive pattern of grandiosity, need for admiration, and lack of empathy, with at least five of nine specified features. Rumlow meets several (grandiose sense of self-importance, belief in being special, sense of entitlement, lack of empathy, arrogance) but **fails the structural test**: a primary NPD subject is organized around the *self* as supreme value and cannot durably submit to another's authority without continuous narcissistic injury. Rumlow has subordinated himself to the Red Skull for the entire adult life without observable injury. His grandiosity is structurally *enclosed within* the Skull's larger grandiosity; he is content to be the right hand, has never made a documented bid for the top seat, and shows none of the chronic envy-and-devaluation cycle that characterizes NPD's relations to authority figures. The Skull is not idealized-then-devalued; he is idealized continuously across decades.

The technically correct framing is **malignant narcissism as a descriptor within an ASPD frame**, per Kernberg — the syndrome of antisocial PD, narcissistic features, paranoid traits, and ego-syntonic aggression — rather than a separate NPD diagnosis. **Differential resolved.**

### 4.6.2 Not Borderline Personality Disorder

BPD requires identity disturbance, affective instability, chronic emptiness, frantic efforts to avoid abandonment, intense unstable relationships with idealization-devaluation, impulsivity in damaging domains, suicidal/self-harming behavior, inappropriate intense anger, transient stress-related paranoid/dissociative symptoms. Rumlow has **stable** identity (anti-borderline), **stable** affect at baseline (anti-borderline), no documented emptiness, no abandonment-avoidance behavior (he does not fear loss of the Skull because he does not psychologically permit the possibility), no idealization-devaluation cycling, no self-directed harm. He has intense anger, but it is *characterological hostility*, not BPD-pattern dyscontrol. **Ruled out cleanly.**

### 4.6.3 Not Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder

This rule-out requires care because the trauma exposure is objectively massive: the disfigurement burn, multiple gunshot wounds, the death/return of the Skull, the imprisonment in Pleasant Hill (with associated identity rewriting), repeated near-death engagements.

PTSD requires (a) exposure to a qualifying stressor, (b) intrusion symptoms (memories, dreams, flashbacks, psychological/physiological reactivity to cues), (c) avoidance of stimuli associated with the trauma, (d) negative alterations in cognitions and mood, (e) marked alterations in arousal and reactivity.

Exposure: trivially met. Every other cluster: **not met.**

- *Intrusion:* no documented intrusive memories, no nightmares (he sleeps adequately, by available evidence), no flashback phenomena, no exaggerated reactivity to trauma cues. The mask, which would in a PTSD-positive subject be a continuous cue to the burn event, functions for him as an emblem rather than a trigger.
- *Avoidance:* he actively seeks the categories of stimulus that produced his injuries — combat, fire, the presence of the Skull — rather than avoiding them.
- *Negative alterations in cognition and mood:* no persistent negative beliefs about self, others, or the world (his beliefs are stable and ego-syntonic); no persistent negative emotional state; no diminished interest in significant activities; no detachment from others (he was already detached; no *change* from a pre-trauma baseline); no inability to experience positive emotion (he experiences his positive emotions — satisfaction in a clean kill, possessive warmth toward Sin — with the same fluency before and after the trauma).
- *Arousal and reactivity:* no irritable behavior or angry outbursts in excess of his baseline (which is already saturated); no hypervigilance beyond tactically-appropriate vigilance; no exaggerated startle; sleep and concentration preserved.

The deeper reason PTSD does not develop in him: **PTSD requires a pre-trauma self that the trauma threatens to invalidate.** The shattered-assumptions model (Janoff-Bulman) is the canonical framing — trauma overwhelms when it contradicts core beliefs about safety, meaning, and self-worth. Rumlow's core beliefs are that the world is a slaughterhouse, that the strong consume the weak, and that he is among the strong. Being burned, shot, imprisoned, or nearly killed does not contradict any of these beliefs; it confirms them. Trauma cannot shatter a worldview that already predicted it. **PTSD ruled out, with formulation.**

### 4.6.4 Not Acute Stress Disorder, Adjustment Disorder

By extension of the above, no episodic stress-related disorder has ever crystallized. Pleasant Hill is the closest case — forced identity substitution by the Kobik cosmic cube — and even there, on restoration, he resumes baseline functioning within an extremely short interval and shows no residual adjustment-disorder picture. **Ruled out.**

### 4.6.5 Not a Primary Psychotic Disorder

No evidence of


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT: BROCK RUMLOW (CROSSBONES)

*Compiled from longitudinal observation of operational footage, after-action debriefs of survivors, surveillance intercepts, prisoner interviews (Diamondback, captured Skull-Cell personnel), and direct combat encounter reports across the entire 1989-present canon record. Cross-referenced against §3-5 of the principal workup.*

This atlas is organized by condition-state. For each state: somatic baseline, kinesic signature, vocal signature, decision-pattern, and characteristic micro-tells. Where the mask is in continuous wear (post-disfigurement), pre-mask data is retained because the underlying face behavior persists in eye, mouth-aperture, and neck movement, and because mask-era body-tells inherit directly from pre-mask body-tells. The man underneath has not changed; only the aperture through which he is observed has narrowed.

---

## I. CONDITION: BASELINE / CALM / OFF-OPERATION

The deceptive state. Most surveillance subjects are *most themselves* at rest; Rumlow at rest is most legibly the predator he is, because he stops bothering to perform anything.

**Somatic.** Resting heart rate estimated mid-50s based on recovery curves observed after sustained combat (he is back to talking-normal within thirty to forty seconds of a full-effort engagement, a recovery rate consistent with a well-conditioned operator in his forties). Posture is *occupying* — he takes the seat with the wall behind him and the door in his sightline without appearing to have chosen it, the choice having been made before he entered the room. Weight forward on the balls of the feet even seated, knees apart at roughly sixty degrees, hands either on thighs or holding something he could throw (cup, knife, magazine). He does not slouch. He does not cross his legs. He does not put his back to glass.

**Kinesic.** Economy of motion is the dominant signature. He does not gesture while talking. He does not fidget. His head moves on a slow, deliberate pan — eyes lead, head follows, never the reverse — that registers a room in roughly three sweeps and then settles. When he is genuinely *at rest*, the resting position of his hands is **palms-down on the thighs, fingers slightly spread**, a position that allows immediate weapon draw or strike launch from any direction. He does not clasp his hands. He does not steeple. Steepling requires a sense of being observed-as-thinker, which he does not perform.

**Vocal.** Lower register than his combat voice, slower cadence, mid-volume. Brooklyn substrate audible — flattened vowels, dropped terminal consonants, the rhythm of someone who grew up needing to be heard over a crowd and never quite shed the projection. He uses sentence fragments more than full sentences when relaxed. He laughs rarely and the laugh is a single exhaled syllable, not a sustained sound.

**Decision-pattern at rest.** He triages. Calm time is used to inventory: which subordinates are slipping, which ammunition is short, which routes have been compromised since last run. He does not "rest" in the recreational sense; rest is administrative. There is no documented hobby, no recreational reading, no music preference established in record, no consumption of art. The closest thing to leisure observable is *weapon maintenance*, which he conducts with a meditative regularity (see §III intimacy-with-objects).

**Micro-tells.**
- Right thumb across the pad of the right index finger, a slow back-and-forth: the **trigger-check tell**, present even when unarmed. Surfaces most in conversation he finds tedious.
- When listening to someone he respects (Skull, Sin), the head tilts five to ten degrees to the dominant ear and stays there for the duration. With anyone else, the head stays square.
- He smells food before he eats it. Not theatrically — a single intake at fork-height. Carry-over from periods of operational poisoning risk; has become reflex.
- He does not drink the first drink poured for him in any setting where he did not pour it himself. He waits one beat, watches, then drinks. The beat is short enough that most observers miss it.

---

## II. CONDITION: PRE-OPERATIONAL / STAGING

The state immediately preceding violence he has planned. Distinguishable from calm by a *narrowing*.

**Somatic.** Respiration deepens and slows further — the **box-breath pattern** familiar from special-operations conditioning: four-in, four-hold, four-out, four-hold. He does not visibly count; the pattern is internalized. Pupil dilation noted in pre-mask footage even in normal light. He warms his hands by working them — slow open-close cycles, knuckle rolls, wrist circles — but only the hands. No shoulder rolls, no neck cracks; theatrical loosening is for amateurs.

**Kinesic.** Movement becomes *more* economical, not less. Where the calm Rumlow will turn his whole head to look, the staging Rumlow moves only the eyes. He stops smelling food. He stops the trigger-check tell because the trigger is no longer abstract. He performs a final weapons-check sequence in invariant order: primary, secondary, blade, secondary-blade, demo, comms, mask seal. The sequence has been observed identical across at least a dozen documented operations spanning fifteen years. Variance in the sequence would be a meaningful flag.

**Vocal.** He goes *quieter*, not louder. Pre-operational Rumlow speaks in clipped imperatives, three to five words, and stops talking entirely about ninety seconds before contact. Subordinates have learned that his silence in the last two minutes before a breach means he is already inside the next room in his head.
